### [1] [Towards Process Mining Use Case Map Models with PM4Py-UCM](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04350v2)
*Daniel Amyot*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了PM4Py-UCM，一个开源工具扩展，使UCM模型成为流程发现的一等输出，支持分层分解和可配置映射，并通过事件日志验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织系统数据量增加，早期需求工程需要更基于证据的方法，但现有流程挖掘输出（如Petri网、BPMN）与URN标准（如UCM）之间存在鸿沟。

Method: 开发PM4Py-UCM扩展，包含UCM发现流水线、分层分解策略、可配置执行者映射和jUCMNav导出器，并通过公开和合成事件日志进行验证。

Result: 展示了相同行为在不同执行者抽象和分解策略下的渲染效果，验证了工具能够保留模型结构并支持模型驱动RE。

Conclusion: PM4Py-UCM使流程挖掘能够生成UCM模型，从而弥合数据与需求工程之间的差距，为模型驱动RE提供实用工具。

中文摘要：鉴于组织系统中可用数据量的增加，早期需求工程（RE）活动有比以往任何时候都更基于证据的机会。流程挖掘（PM）已被使用二十多年，用于从此类数据中提取的事件日志发现和分析现状流程模型，其输出形式通常是Petri网、直接跟随图或BPMN模型。本文旨在使ITU-T的用户需求符号（URN）中的用例图（UCM）模型成为流程发现的一等输出，以便将挖掘的行为用于基于URN的建模、分析和管理活动。本文贡献并展示了PM4Py-UCM，一个对现有PM4Py Python库的开源扩展。这个新工具贡献了1）一个UCM发现流水线，2）产生嵌套UCM模型的分层分解策略，3）UCM和BPMN可视化的可配置执行者映射，以及4）一个导出到URN工具（jUCMNav）的导出器，该导出器在往返过程中保留挖掘的模型。使用公开和合成的事件日志，本文展示了相同行为如何在不同的执行者抽象和分解策略下呈现，并讨论了PM如何成为模型驱动RE的实用工具。

Original abstract: Given the increasing amount of data available in organizational systems, there is an opportunity for early requirements engineering (RE) activities to be better based on evidence than ever before. Process mining (PM) has been used for over two decades to discover and analyze as-is process models from event logs extracted from such data, with outputs often in the form of Petri Nets, directly-follows graphs, or BPMN models. This paper aims to make Use Case Map (UCM) models, from ITU-T's User Requirements Notation (URN), a first-class output of process discovery, so that mined behavior can be used in URN-based modeling, analysis, and management activities. This paper contributes and illustrates PM4Py-UCM, an open-source extension to the existing PM4Py Python library. This new tool contributes 1) a UCM discovery pipeline, 2) hierarchical decomposition strategies producing nested UCM models, 3) configurable performer mappings for UCM and BPMN visualizations, and 4) an exporter to a URN tool (jUCMNav) that preserves the mined model under round-trip. Using public and synthetic event logs, the paper showcases how the same behavior is rendered under different performer abstractions and decomposition strategies, and discusses how PM can become a practical instrument for model-driven RE.

</details>


### [2] [Beyond Single-Policy: Evaluating Composed Organization-Specific Policy Alignment in LLM Chatbots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04394v1)
*Yingjie Liu,Yongxiang Hu,Xuan Wang,Yilun Li,Yunlei Wei,Xiaoyu Wang,Yangfan Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出COPAL工具，自动评估聊天机器人的复合政策对齐，发现现有模型存在33.1%的复合政策错误率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界聊天机器人面临复合政策违规问题，但现有基准未覆盖。

Method: 通过分析真实用户查询，构建交互模式和显式处理契约，自动化生成触发复合政策失败的查询。

Result: 在9个模型上测试，复合政策查询平均错误率33.1%。

Conclusion: 复合政策对齐是聊天机器人部署中的重要问题，需要进一步研究。

中文摘要：大型语言模型聊天机器人越来越多地部署在医疗、金融和公共服务等组织环境中。因此，评估政策对齐对于可靠的聊天机器人部署至关重要。通过分析真实世界的用户查询，我们发现在各种聊天机器人中，复合政策违规普遍存在，但被现有基准所忽视。本文提出了COPAL，一个用于评估聊天机器人中复合政策对齐的自动化工具。COPAL通过经验推导的交互模式和显式处理契约，高效生成触发聊天机器人复合政策失败的查询。由COPAL生成的查询暴露了显著的查询处理失败：在9个服务的模型中，复合政策查询平均产生33.1%的错误率，表明复合政策对齐需要进一步研究。

Original abstract: Large language model chatbots are increasingly deployed in organizational settings such as healthcare, finance, and public services. Evaluating policy alignment is therefore critical to reliable chatbot deployment. By analyzing real-world user queries, we identify composed-policy violation is prevalent in various chatbots but overlooked by existing benchmarks. This paper present COPAL, an automated tool for evaluating composed-policy alignment in chatbots. COPAL efficiently generates queries that trigger composed-policy failures in chatbots via empirically derived interaction patterns and explicit handling contracts. Queries generated by COPAL expose substantial query handling failures: across 9 served models, composed-policy queries yield a 33.1% error rate on average, indicating that composed-policy alignment warrants further investigation.

</details>


### [3] [Context-as-AI-Service: Surfacing Cross-File Dependency Chains for LLM-Generated Developer Documentation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04397v3)
*Ameya Gawde,Vyzantinos Repantis,Harshvardhan Singh,Lucy Moys*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CAIS是一个检索层，帮助LLM代理在编写和维护文档时有效追踪跨文件依赖，通过案例研究证明其能发现基线遗漏的问题并减少时间和令牌消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理在编写和维护开发者文档时，依赖链不直观且难以追踪，即使有更多上下文文件，代理仍需决定追踪哪些依赖，导致有用性和准确性受限。

Method: 提出Context-as-AI-Service (CAIS)，通过索引源代码、API参考和上游文档，结合关键词与语义搜索，为LLM代理提供可查询的检索层，以帮助发现跨文件证据。

Result: 在API参考审查中，CAIS代理发现基线遗漏的4个问题（2个事实错误、2个未充分描述的注释）；在教程验证中发现3个新问题（1个可执行错误、1个API改进、2个缺失前提条件）；同时减少22%-34%的挂钟时间和输入令牌使用量。

Conclusion: CAIS通过提供针对性的检索层，有效提升了LLM代理在文档相关的任务中的准确性和效率，能够发现非明显依赖链中的问题，并减少资源消耗。

中文摘要：LLM代理越来越多地编写和维护开发者文档，但有用性和准确性通常依赖于不明显的依赖链。即使有更多文件在上下文中，代理仍必须决定追踪哪些跨文件依赖。我们提出Context-as-AI-Service（CAIS），一个检索层，LLM代理在审查或生成文档时查询它以查找代码库中的证据。CAIS索引源代码、API参考和上游文档，然后使代理能够通过结合关键词和语义搜索的工具调用来查询索引。我们使用Claude Sonnet 4.6在一个生产SDK上通过两个案例研究评估CAIS：改进核心源文件中的API参考注释和验证LLM生成的教程。在两个研究中，基线已经具有普通的仓库工具，如文件读取、关键词搜索和符号导航。CAIS在其上添加了一个检索层，因此比较隔离了添加的检索而不是基本的仓库访问。在API参考审查中，CAIS增强的代理产生了与基线相同的5个缺失文档修复，并发现了基线遗漏的4个发现：2个跨文件事实错误和2个未充分描述的API注释。在教程验证中，它发现了1个可执行错误、1个API使用改进和2个基线管道未捕获的缺失前提条件。这些发现需要追踪跨工具文件、框架内部、使用示例、测试和组件创建逻辑的非明显依赖链。在每个条件下运行五次后，添加CAIS在两个任务中减少了22%到34%的挂钟时间，并降低了输入令牌使用量。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly write and maintain developer documentation, but usefulness and accuracy often rely on dependency chains that are not obvious to follow. Even with more files in context, the agent must still decide which cross-file dependencies to trace. We present Context-as-AI-Service (CAIS), a retrieval layer that LLM agents query to find evidence across the codebase as they review or generate documentation. CAIS indexes source code, API references, and upstream documentation, then enables agents to query the index through tool calls that combine keyword and semantic search. We evaluate CAIS in two case studies using Claude Sonnet 4.6 on a production SDK: improving API reference comments in a core source file and validating an LLM-generated tutorial. In both studies, the baseline already had ordinary repository tools such as file reads, keyword search, and symbol navigation. CAIS adds a retrieval layer on top, so the comparison isolates added retrieval rather than basic repository access. In the API-reference review, the CAIS-augmented agent produced the same 5 missing-documentation fixes as the baseline and surfaced 4 findings the baseline missed: 2 cross-file factual errors and 2 underspecified API comments. In the tutorial validation, it surfaced 1 executable bug, 1 API-usage improvement, and 2 missing prerequisites that the baseline pipeline did not catch. These findings required tracing non-obvious dependency chains across utility files, framework internals, usage examples, tests, and component-creation logic. Over five runs per condition, adding CAIS reduced wall-clock time by 22% to 34% across the two tasks and lowered input-token usage.

</details>


### [4] [DeployBench: Benchmarking LLM Agents for Research Artifact Deployment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05238v1)
*Yuanli Wang,Yaoyao Qian,Yue Zhang,Hanhan Zhou,Jindan Huang,Tianfu Fu,Qiuyang Mang,Huanzhi Mao,Wenhao Chai,Wendong Fan,Liqiang Jing*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出DeployBench，一个涵盖多领域研究工件部署的基准，揭示当前LLM代理在自主环境部署上的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有环境设置基准未覆盖研究工件部署的完整范围（多语言工具链、系统级依赖、遗留兼容性），导致从零搭建环境成为瓶颈。

Method: 构建包含51个多领域任务的DeployBench，每个任务由隐藏流水线验证，使用OpenHands评估四种LLM。

Result: LLM通过率7.8%-51.0%，失败主要因代理自我停止（97/154），其验证目标与任务要求不符。

Conclusion: DeployBench凸显了当前代理与自主部署的差距，为科学研究代理提供现实测试床。

中文摘要：LLM代理在软件工程和机器学习研究任务上取得了快速进展，但这些进展通常假设能够访问一个可运行的执行环境。对于与已发表论文一同发布的研究工件，从一台全新的机器上设置这样的环境仍然是一个主要瓶颈。现有的环境设置基准测试并未涵盖研究工件部署的全部范围，这涉及多语言工具链、超越容器的系统级依赖（例如GPU/CUDA和内核配置）以及遗留工件兼容性。我们引入了DeployBench，这是一个涵盖AI/ML、计算机系统和科学计算领域的51个研究工件部署任务的多领域基准，覆盖了所有这些维度。每个任务通过一个隐藏的流水线进行验证，该流水线执行论文指定的实验并检查其输出。使用OpenHands评估四种最先进的LLM，通过率从7.8%到51.0%不等。失败主要由完成判断问题主导：154次失败中有97次是代理终止的自我停止，其中代理的事先完成检查验证了与论文特定任务所需不同的或较弱的目标。DeployBench突出了当前代理与自主部署之间的差距，并为科学研究代理提供了一个现实的测试平台。

Original abstract: LLM agents have made rapid progress on software engineering and ML research tasks, but these advances often assume access to a working runnable environment. For research artifacts released alongside published papers, setting up such an environment from a fresh machine remains a major bottleneck. Existing environment setup benchmarks do not cover the full scope of research artifact deployment, which involves multi-language toolchains, system-level dependencies beyond containers (e.g. GPU/CUDA and kernel configurations), and legacy artifact compatibility. We introduce DeployBench, a multi-domain benchmark of 51 research-artifact deployment tasks spanning AI/ML, computer systems, and scientific computing, covering all these dimensions. Each task is verified by a hidden pipeline that executes the paper's designated experiment and checks its outputs. Evaluating four state-of-the-art LLMs with OpenHands yields pass-rates from 7.8% - 51.0% . Failures are dominated by a completion-judgment problem: 97 of 154 are agent-terminated self-stops, where the agent's pre-finish checks validate a different or weaker target than the paper-specific task requires. DeployBench highlights the gap between current agents and autonomous deployment, and offers a realistic testbed for scientific research agents.

</details>


### [5] [Extraction and Search in Rocq: Theorems, Definitions and Their dependencies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04704v1)
*Jian Fang,Yingfei Xiong*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Rocq定理提取与分析工具TheoremExtr，从32个开源项目中提取大量定理、定义及依赖关系，并开发了跨项目相似性搜索网站。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Rocq搜索命令局限于导入模块内的定理，且缺乏高效工具提取全面的定理信息（如名称、陈述和依赖关系），限制了证明辅助和工具开发。

Method: 开发TheoremExtr工具，支持从解析阶段和运行时提取定理、依赖关系和定义；构建网站实现跨项目相似性搜索。

Result: 从32个开源项目中提取了71,795个定理及其依赖关系，以及27,481个定义及其类型。

Conclusion: TheoremExtr有效支持定理的搜索、提取和分析，有助于提升Rocq证明效率与工具生态建设。

中文摘要：Rocq (Coq) 现已广泛应用于各个领域，包括软件验证和数学证明。在证明新定理时，用户通常需要搜索并应用已证明的定理来辅助当前的证明过程。然而，当前的搜索命令仅限于已导入模块的环境，无法搜索该范围之外的定理。此外，工具开发人员和研究人员可能希望获取定理的详细信息，例如定理的名称、陈述和依赖关系。但目前没有用户友好且高效的工具可用于从Rocq项目中提取全面信息。我们介绍了一种Rocq定理提取和分析工具TheoremExtr，它能够分析定理构成，并从解析阶段和运行时提取定理、依赖关系和定义。我们从Rocq社区的32个开源项目中提取了71,795个定理及其依赖关系。此外，我们还从这些项目中提取了27,481个定义及其类型。我们还开发了一个网站，支持定理和定义的跨项目相似性搜索。该工具可在https://github.com/Rw1nd/TheoremExtr获取，搜索网站可在https://lemmasearch.com访问。

Original abstract: Rocq (Coq) are now widely used in various fields, including software verification and mathematical proofs. When proving a new theorem, users often need to search and apply proven theorems to assist the current proof process. However, the current search command is limited to the environment of imported modules and cannot search for theorems outside of this scope. Furthermore, tool developers and researchers may want to obtain detailed information about theorems, such as theorem's names, statements, and dependencies. But there are currently no user-friendly and efficient tools available for extracting comprehensive information from Rocq projects. We introduce a Rocq theorem extraction and analysis tool, TheoremExtr, which is capable of analyzing theorem composition and extracting theorems, dependencies, and definitions from both parsing phase and runtime. We extracted 71,795 theorems and their dependencies from 32 open-source projects from the Rocq community. In addition, we extracted 27,481 definitions and their types among these projects. We also developed a website that supports cross-project similarity search for theorems and definitions. The tool is available at https://github.com/Rw1nd/TheoremExtr, and the search website is available at https://lemmasearch.com.

</details>


### [6] [The State of Peer Review in Empirical Software Engineering: A Community Survey on Review Load, Quality, and GenAI Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04716v1)
*Justus Bogner,Roberto Verdecchia*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过问卷调查了解ESE社区同行评审现状，包括审稿负荷、质量感知、LLM工具使用及改进建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同行评审系统近年来持续恶化，投稿量增加、工作负荷高、生成式AI带来新问题，因此需要了解社区对评审现状的看法。

Method: 采用问卷调查方法，收集了120份来自ESE社区成员的回复。

Result: 主要结果包括：社区成员感知的审稿负荷、评审质量与常见问题、LLM工具在评审中的使用情况，以及社区对改进评审系统的建议。

Conclusion: 研究期望这些社区意见能推动关于评审系统改进的基于证据的讨论。

中文摘要：科学同行评审系统在过去几年中一直在缓慢恶化，而且不仅仅是在经验软件工程（ESE）研究领域。增加的投稿数量、高工作负荷以及生成式人工智能的使用及其相关问题，使得系统中的许多裂痕更加明显。为了更好地了解ESE社区中同行评审的现状，我们进行了一项问卷调查，共收集了120份回复。我们报告了（i）社区成员感知的审稿负荷，（ii）审稿质量感知以及评审中常见的挑战和问题，（iii）基于LLM的工具在评审过程中的使用，以及（iv）社区对改进同行评审系统的建议。我们希望这些社区意见能够促进更多基于证据的讨论，讨论人们希望看到评审系统如何向更好的方向改变。

Original abstract: The scientific peer review system has been slowly deteriorating over the last years, and not just within empirical software engineering (ESE) research. Increased submission numbers, high workload, and the rise of generative AI use with all its associated issues have made many cracks in the system more visible. To get a better understanding of the current state of peer review in the ESE community, we conducted a questionnaire survey, which accumulated 120 responses. We report on (i) the perceived review load of community members, (ii) review quality perception as well as frequent challenges for and issues with reviews, (iii) the use of LLM-based tools in the reviewing process, and (iv) the community's suggestions for improving the peer review system. We hope that these community opinions can facilitate more evidence-based discussions about how people want to see the review system change for the better.

</details>


### [7] [Revisiting Vul-RAG: Reproducibility and Replicability of RAG-based Vulnerability Detection with Open-Weight Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04739v1)
*Sabrina Kaniewski,Fabian Schmidt,Tobias Heer*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对Vul-RAG（一个基于RAG的漏洞检测框架）的可重复性研究发现，其结论在本地部署下可复现，但存在微小偏差；所有模型性能均在成对准确率0.30左右达到平台期，表明仅提升模型能力无法突破该瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 依赖专有模型和API的漏洞检测方法的可重复性和可再现性未被探索，现有结果是否普遍适用未知。

Method: 使用开源基线模型在本地复现Vul-RAG结果，并扩展到多种最新开源LLM（代码专用、通用、推理模型）进行评估。

Result: 各模型性能在成对准确率约0.30处达到平台期，即使更新模型也未显著提升。

Conclusion: Vul-RAG发现可复现但存在偏差，模型能力提升无法突破性能瓶颈，需考虑检测效果与模型规模的权衡。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在自动化软件漏洞检测方面显示出强大潜力，特别是在检索增强生成（RAG）设置中。然而，对于依赖专有模型和API的方法，可重复性和可再现性仍然很大程度上未被探索，这引发了一个问题：报告的结果是否具有普遍性，还是主要取决于特定的模型选择。在这项工作中，我们对Vul-RAG进行了可重复性研究，Vul-RAG是一个基于RAG的源代码漏洞检测框架，它通过高层漏洞知识增强LLM。我们首先使用报告的开源基线模型在完全本地和开放权重的设置中复现结果。然后，我们将评估扩展到一组多样化的最新开源LLM，包括代码专用、通用和推理模型，参数规模各异。结果证实，Vul-RAG的发现可以本地部署复现，但存在微小偏差。在所有评估的模型中，我们观察到性能平台期，大约为0.30的成对准确率（即同时正确分类漏洞函数和修补函数的代码对）。值得注意的是，即使对于更新更先进的模型，这个平台期仍然存在，表明仅通过提高模型容量并不能显著提升性能。最后，我们讨论了检测效果、模型能力和模型规模之间的实际影响和权衡。实现和评估工件可在https://github.com/hs-esslingen-it-security/revisiting-Vul-RAG公开获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong potential for automated software vulnerability detection, particularly in retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) settings. However, for approaches relying on proprietary models and APIs, reproducibility and replicability remain largely unexplored, raising the question of whether reported results generalize or depend primarily on specific model choices. In this work, we present a reproducibility study of Vul-RAG, a RAG-based framework for source code vulnerability detection that enhances LLMs with high-level vulnerability knowledge. We first replicate the results in a fully local and open-weights setting using the reported open-weight baseline models. We then extend the evaluation to a diverse set of recent open-weight LLMs, including code-specialized, general-purpose, and reasoning models of varying parameter sizes. The results confirm that the findings of Vul-RAG are reproducible under local deployment, but with minor deviations. Across all evaluated models, we observe a performance plateau at approximately 0.30 pairwise accuracy (code pairs for which both the vulnerable and the patched function are correctly classified). Notably, this plateau persists even for more recent and advanced models, indicating that improvements in model capacity alone do not substantially enhance performance. Finally, we discuss practical implications and trade-offs between detection effectiveness, model capabilities, and model scale. Implementation and evaluation artifacts are publicly available at https://github.com/hs-esslingen-it-security/revisiting-Vul-RAG.

</details>


### [8] [UModel: An Agent-Ready Observability Data Modeling Method at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04799v1)
*Changhua Pei,Zheyuan Li,Zexin Wang,Hang Cui,Xiaohui Nie,Qi Zhou,Fang Situ,Cheng Zhang,Xin Zhang,Xidao Wen,Gaogang Xie,Jingjing Li,Dan Pei*

TL;DR: 提出UModel统一本体论框架，将可观测性从数据中心转向对象中心建模，通过语义图标准化异构数据，并引入U-SPL查询接口，使智能体能自主探索系统，提升根因分析精度8%，在阿里云大规模部署。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可观测框架存在数据孤岛、模式不兼容和语义元数据不足，阻碍了基于LLM的智能体进行有效的根因分析。

Method: 提出UModel统一本体论框架，构建虚拟本体层，将异构数据、实体和知识标准化为对象并通过语义图互联；同时引入U-SPL管道查询接口，支持智能体自主探索系统拓扑和关联多模态数据。

Result: 在AIOps 2025挑战赛数据集上，根因定位精度提升8%；在阿里云部署一年，服务数万用户，支撑百万级QPS，查询延迟亚秒级。

Conclusion: UModel提供了可扩展的建模框架，通过改进数据组织显著提升下游RCA任务准确性，并在大规模实际部署中验证了高性能。

中文摘要：当网络化系统故障发生时，利用可观测数据自动执行根因分析（RCA）对于确保网络化系统的可靠性至关重要。最近，基于大语言模型的智能体通过高级推理和自主探索在自动化这一诊断过程中展现出潜力。然而，现有的可观测框架仍然陈旧，表现为碎片化的数据孤岛、不兼容的模式以及不足的语义元数据，这阻碍了智能体建立有效RCA所需的复杂关系。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了UModel，一个统一的本体论框架，将可观测性从以数据为中心建模转变为以对象为中心建模。UModel构建了一个虚拟本体层，在该层中，异构遥测、实体和专家知识被标准化为对象，并通过语义图相互连接。此外，我们引入了U-SPL，一种基于管道的查询接口，使智能体能够自主探索系统拓扑并关联多模态数据。通过使用UModel对“AIOps 2025挑战赛”数据集进行重新建模，根因定位的准确率提升了8%，这表明增强的数据组织可以显著提高下游任务的准确性。UModel提供了一个可扩展的建模框架，在阿里云部署超过一年期间，已服务数万用户，支撑每秒数百万次操作，并实现亚秒级查询延迟。

Original abstract: When networked system failures occur, automatically performing Root Cause Analysis (RCA) using observability data is critical for ensuring networked system reliability. Recently, LLM-based agents have shown promise for automating this diagnosis process through advanced reasoning and autonomous exploration. However, existing observability frameworks remain archaic, characterized by fragmented data silos, incompatible schemas, and insufficient semantic metadata, preventing agents from establishing the complex relationships required for effective RCA. To address these challenges, we present UModel, a unified ontological framework that shifts observability from data-centric to object-centric modeling. UModel constructs a virtual ontological layer where heterogeneous telemetry, entities, and expert knowledge are standardized as objects and interconnected via semantic graphs. In addition, we introduce U-SPL, a pipeline-based query interface that enables agents to autonomously explore system topologies and correlate multimodal data. By re-modeling the "AIOps 2025 Challenge" dataset using UModel, the precision of root cause localization improved by 8%, demonstrating that enhanced data organization can significantly increase the accuracy of downstream tasks. UModel provides a scalable modeling framework that, in its deployment at Alibaba Cloud for more than one year, has served tens of thousands of users, sustained millions of operations per second, and delivered sub-second query latency.

### [9] [SWE-InfraBench: Evaluating Language Models on Cloud Infrastructure Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05249v1)
*Natalia Tarasova,Enrique Balp-Straffon,Aleksei Iancheruk,Yevhenii Sielskyi,Nikita Kozodoi,Liam H. Byrne,Jack Butler,Dayuan Jiang,Marcin Czelej,Andrew Ang,Yash Shah,Roi Blanco,Sergei Ivanov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了SWE-InfraBench，一个评估LLM在真实IaC增量代码编辑能力的基准，发现当前顶级模型成功率不足35%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从数十个真实AWS CDK代码库中构建包含自然语言指令和测试用例的数据集，要求LLM基于现有代码进行修改，通过测试用例判断成功。

Result: 最佳模型Sonnet 3.7仅有34%成功率，DeepSeek R1仅24%，表明当前LLM在IaC任务中表现有限。

Conclusion: LLM在IaC增量代码编辑任务上能力不足，需要进一步提升对云资源依赖和实现模式的推理能力。

中文摘要：在云计算中构建基础设施即代码（IaC）是一项关键任务，支撑着现代软件系统的可靠性、可扩展性和安全性。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在软件工程领域取得了显著进展——这已在许多专门基准测试中得到证明——但它们在开发IaC方面的能力仍未得到充分探索。与现有的IaC基准主要侧重于声明式范式（如Terraform）并从零开始生成整个代码库不同，我们的基准反映了使用命令式工具（如AWS CDK）在企业开发中常见的增量代码编辑。我们提出了SWE-InfraBench，这是一个从数十个真实世界IaC代码库中收集的多样化评估数据集，挑战LLM在AWS CDK仓库中执行现实的代码修改。每个示例要求模型根据自然语言指令对现有代码库进行更改，成功与否由是否通过提供的测试用例决定。这些任务需要超越传统代码生成挑战的复杂推理，涉及云资源依赖关系和实现模式。我们的评估结果揭示了当前LLM的显著局限性，表明即使是最先进的系统也在许多任务上挣扎——最佳模型Sonnet 3.7仅在34%的情况下成功，而专门推理模型如DeepSeek R1仅达到24%的成功率。SWE-InfraBench数据集可在以下网址获取：https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/64e59070fd51c0278560b01eb5dc4f3c447d5268cdabe5a350d2969e4413fea5

Original abstract: Building infrastructure-as-code (IaC) in cloud computing is a critical task, underpinning the reliability, scalability, and security of modern software systems. Despite the remarkable progress of large language models (LLMs) in software engineering -- demonstrated across many dedicated benchmarks -- their capabilities in developing IaC remain underexplored. Unlike existing IaC benchmarks that predominantly center on declarative paradigms such as Terraform and involve generating entire codebases from scratch, our benchmark reflects the incremental code edits common in enterprise development with imperative tools like the AWS CDK. We present SWE-InfraBench, a diverse evaluation dataset sourced from dozens of real-world IaC codebases that challenge LLMs to perform realistic code modifications in AWS CDK repositories. Each example requires models to implement changes to existing codebases based on natural language instructions, with success determined by passing provided test cases. These tasks demand sophisticated reasoning about cloud resource dependencies and implementation patterns beyond conventional code generation challenges. Our evaluation results reveal significant limitations in current LLMs showing that even state-of-the-art systems struggle with many tasks -- the best model, Sonnet 3.7, succeeds in only 34\% of cases, while specialized reasoning models like DeepSeek R1 achieve just 24% success. The SWE-InfraBench dataset is available at: https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/64e59070fd51c0278560b01eb5dc4f3c447d5268cdabe5a350d2969e4413fea5

### [10] [Towards Persistent Case-Based Memory for Autonomous Data Science: A CBR-Augmented R&D-Agent with a Locally Deployable Small Language Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05250v1)
*Felix Stocker*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出CBR增强的R&D-Agent，将持久化CBR层集成到微软框架中，首次评估Gemma 4作为自主数据科学智能体骨干，在两个Kaggle任务中CBR提升了准确率并降低了方差，且案例重用以概念指导为主。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主数据科学智能体多依赖云模型且缺乏持久记忆，同时小语言模型作为本地骨干的可行性尚未验证。

Method: 将CBR层集成到R&D-Agent框架，使用Gemma 4 31B Dense作为骨干，通过外科手术子类覆盖R&D循环的三个阶段，案例含可执行代码快照和质量元数据，采用五门质量过滤器和启发式重用检测机制。

Result: 在Spaceship Titanic上CBR准确率0.8147高于基线0.8098（d=-1.41），方差更低；重用检测显示高语义相似度（0.882）和低代码指纹相似度（0.305），表明概念性知识迁移。

Conclusion: CBR增强的SLM智能体在本地部署场景中可行，能提升性能并降低方差，且案例重用倾向于概念指导而非复制代码。

中文摘要：大多数表现最好的自主数据科学智能体依赖于前沿云模型，并且缺乏持久化的跨会话记忆。本文解决了两个未充分探索的空白：（1）将形式化、质量控制的基于案例的推理（CBR）案例库与可执行代码工件相结合，其中案例记录是符号化的；以及（2）小语言模型（SLM）作为可本地部署的智能体骨干的可行性尚未经过测试。我们提出了CBR增强的R&D-Agent，将持久化CBR层集成到微软的R&D-Agent框架中，并为Gemma 4 31B Dense定制了后端——这是首次公开的将Gemma 4作为自主数据科学智能体骨干的端到端评估。CBR层通过一个由单个环境变量切换的外科手术子类覆盖了R&D循环的三个阶段。案例以结构化记录的形式存储，包含可执行代码快照和质量元数据；一个五门质量过滤器和一个启发式重用检测机制通过结合嵌入相似性、代码指纹重叠和注入来源来评估知识迁移。在两个Kaggle竞赛（NOMAD 2018, Spaceship Titanic）上进行了评估，每个竞赛使用四个种子和八次改进循环，CBR在Spaceship Titanic上取得了比禁用CBR的基线更高的准确率（0.8147 vs. 0.8098, d = -1.41），且方差显著降低。跨108次检索事件的启发式重用检测显示高语义相关性（平均嵌入相似度0.882）以及可变的结构接近度（平均代码指纹相似度0.305），这与概念指导而非逐字代码复制一致。

Original abstract: Most top-performing autonomous data-science agents rely on frontier cloud models and lack persistent, cross-session memory. This paper addresses two open gaps: (1) the underexplored use of formally structured, quality-controlled Case-Based Reasoning (CBR) case bases coupling symbolic case records with executable code artefacts; and (2) the untested viability of Small Language Models (SLMs) as locally deployable agent backbones. We present CBR-augmented R&D-Agent, integrating a persistent CBR layer into Microsoft's R&D-Agent framework with a custom backend for Gemma 4 31B Dense -- the first published end-to-end evaluation of Gemma 4 as an autonomous data-science agent backbone. The CBR layer overrides three R&D loop phases via a surgical subclass toggled by a single environment variable. Cases are stored as structured records with executable code snapshots and quality metadata; a five-gate quality filter and a heuristic reuse-detection mechanism assess knowledge transfer by combining embedding similarity, code-fingerprint overlap, and injection provenance. Evaluated on two Kaggle competitions (NOMAD 2018, Spaceship Titanic) with four seeds over eight improvement loops each, CBR achieves directionally higher accuracy than the CBR-disabled baseline on Spaceship Titanic (0.8147 vs. 0.8098, d = -1.41) with substantially lower variance. Heuristic reuse detection across 108 retrieval events shows high semantic relevance (mean embedding similarity 0.882) alongside variable structural proximity (mean code-fingerprint similarity 0.305), consistent with conceptual guidance rather than verbatim code copying.

### [11] [From Prompt to Process: a Process Taxonomy and Comparative Assessment of Frameworks Supporting AI Software Development Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04967v1)
*Sanderson Oliveira de Macedo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过定向搜索选择了六个AI开发框架，提出了一个六维流程分类法，并应用于这些框架，发现流程趋同但存在维度覆盖不全的结构权衡，以及重复风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对将AI能力转化为流程的操作框架的系统性分析，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 进行定向主要来源搜索，选择六个框架，提出六维流程分类法（规范、上下文、角色、执行、验证、可移植性）及评分标准，并应用于所选框架及一个样本外案例。

Result: 框架之间存在流程趋同（孤立提示失去中心地位，持久工件等成为关键），但无框架强覆盖全部六维，暴露流程深度与可移植性的权衡；识别出重复风险（规范-代码漂移、过度信任生成工件等）。

Conclusion: 提出以实证评估为重点的研究议程，关注中间质量指标、上下文治理、安装安全性和可重复性。

中文摘要：人工智能编程工具不再仅仅是自动补全或聊天助手：它们将自己组织成开发框架，包含流程、角色、工件和验证。最近的调查绘制了软件工程中的智能体和大型语言模型，但缺少一项以将这些能力转化为流程的操作框架为中心的研究。我们进行了定向的主要来源搜索，具有功能性的纳入标准和影响力测量，并选择了六个框架：GitHub Spec Kit、OpenSpec、BMAD Method、Get Shit Done (GSD)、Spec Kitty 和 Reversa。每个框架通过不同的路径攻击人工智能开发：完整和轻量级的规范驱动开发、智能体驱动的敏捷规划、智能体上的上下文工程、工作树隔离和审查，以及从遗留系统中恢复操作规范。我们的核心贡献是一个六维流程分类法：规范、上下文、角色、执行、验证和可移植性，并配有一个评分标准，使其成为可重复使用的工具。我们将其应用于六个框架和一个样本外案例 Spec-Flow。两个结果突出显示。在已经采用某些流程的框架中，存在趋同性：孤立提示失去中心地位，持久工件、工作契约、可追溯性和人工审查成为减少歧义和协调智能体的机制。没有框架强有力地覆盖所有六个维度，暴露了流程深度与跨智能体可移植性之间的结构权衡。我们还发现了重复出现的风险：规范与代码之间的漂移、对生成工件的过度信任、社区扩展的脆弱性、平台依赖以及缺乏完整流程的基准。我们以实证评估的研究议程结束，重点关注中间质量指标、上下文治理、安装安全性和可重复性。

Original abstract: AI tools for programming are no longer just autocomplete or chat assistants: they organize themselves as development frameworks, with process, roles, artifacts and verification. Recent surveys map agents and LLMs for software engineering, but a study centered on the operational frameworks that turn these capabilities into process is missing. We ran a directed search of primary sources, with a functional inclusion criterion and traction measurement, and selected six frameworks: GitHub Spec Kit, OpenSpec, BMAD Method, Get Shit Done (GSD), Spec Kitty and Reversa. Each attacks AI development through a different path: spec-driven development in full and lightweight variants, agent-driven agile planning, context engineering over the agent, worktree isolation and review, and recovery of operational specifications from legacy systems. Our central contribution is a six-dimension process taxonomy: specification, context, roles, execution, validation and portability, with a scoring rubric that turns it into a replicable instrument. We apply it to the six frameworks and an out-of-sample case, Spec-Flow. Two results stand out. Among frameworks that already adopt some process there is convergence: the isolated prompt loses centrality, and persistent artifacts, work contracts, traceability and human review become mechanisms that reduce ambiguity and coordinate agents. And no framework strongly covers all six dimensions, exposing a structural trade-off between process depth and portability across agents. We also found recurring risks: drift between specification and code, excessive trust in generated artifacts, fragility of community extensions, platform dependence and a lack of benchmarks for the complete process. We close with a research agenda for empirical evaluation, focused on intermediate-quality metrics, context governance, installation security and reproducibility.

</details>


### [12] [Code Lifespan Survival Analysis (CLSA): Predicting the Survival of Source Code Lines Using AST-Aware Mining](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04993v3)
*Pavel Gurov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出CLSA框架，对代码行级删除风险进行生存分析，发现超半数行永不删除，删除行中位寿命95.7天，协变量效应随时间变化，存储库身份影响最大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法以文件或方法粒度预测删除，无法捕捉单行风险；先前行级工作未发现显著预测因子，亟需行级删除风险模型。

Method: 从120个TypeScript仓库挖掘3250万行出生事件，通过5阶段匹配管道去除重构噪声，拟合含15个协变量的Cox比例风险模型，并使用Weibull/Log-Logistic AFT、gamma脆弱性及时间分层界标模型验证稳健性。

Result: 超半数行永不删除（中位未达），删除行中位寿命95.7天；协变量效应呈三个时间区间，行令牌数持续保护（HR=0.80），条件分支从保护转为风险（HR从0.98升至1.21），存储库身份为最大影响因素（脆弱性模型一致性从0.593提升至0.667）。

Conclusion: 行级生存建模可行，产生可解释的静态风险信号，可校准IDE与代码审查中的时间条件风险评分。

中文摘要：背景：预测哪些源代码行将被删除以及何时删除，对于维护、技术债务和审查优先级很重要。现有的MSR方法以文件或方法粒度工作，掩盖了单个语句的风险。目标：我们引入了代码生命周期生存分析（CLSA），这是第一个从协变量建模单行删除风险的框架——而先前的行粒度工作估计了生命周期，但未发现显著的预测因子。CLSA将每一行视为一个右删失主体，并根据结构、上下文和时间协变量估计删除风险；其最强的预测因子可以从一个文件中静态计算（AST结构加上行令牌计数），无需版本历史或缺陷数据。方法：我们从120个开源TypeScript存储库中挖掘了3250万行诞生事件。一个5阶段匹配管道将真实删除与重构噪声分开，防止了830万个虚假死亡。我们拟合了一个包含15个协变量的Cox比例风险模型，并通过Weibull/Log-Logistic AFT、gamma脆弱性和时间分层界标模型检查稳健性。结果：超过一半的行从未被删除（Kaplan-Meier中位数未达到）；在被删除的行中，中位生命周期为95.7天。协变量效应随时间强烈变化，形成三个时期。行令牌计数是一个稳定的保护因素（HR=0.80），随着年龄的增长而轻微增强（三个时期的HR分别为0.87至0.77）。条件分支中的行发生逆转：出生时是保护因素（HR=0.98，0-90天），90天后成为风险因素（HR=1.21）。存储库身份是最大的因素：gamma脆弱性模型（方差theta=1.208）将一致性从0.593提高到0.667，超过了每个结构协变量。结论：行级生存建模是可行的，产生可解释的、主要是静态的风险信号，以及用于IDE和代码审查中时间条件风险评分的校准配方。

Original abstract: Context: Predicting which source lines will be deleted - and when - matters for maintenance, technical debt, and review prioritization. Existing MSR approaches work at file or method granularity, masking individual-statement risk. Objective: We introduce Code Lifespan Survival Analysis (CLSA), the first framework to model individual-line deletion risk from covariates - where prior line-granularity work estimated lifespans but found no significant predictors. CLSA treats each line as a right-censored subject and estimates deletion risk from structural, contextual, and temporal covariates; its strongest predictors are computable statically from one file (AST structure plus line token count), without version history or bug data. Method: We mine 32.5 million line birth events from 120 open-source TypeScript repositories. A 5-stage matching pipeline separates true deletions from refactoring noise, preventing 8.3 million false deaths. We fit a Cox Proportional Hazards model with 15 covariates and check robustness via Weibull/Log-Logistic AFT, gamma frailty, and time-stratified landmark models. Results: Over half of all lines are never deleted (Kaplan-Meier median not reached); among deleted lines the median lifespan is 95.7 days. Covariate effects are strongly time-varying, forming three regimes. Line token count is a steady protective factor (HR=0.80) that strengthens gently with age (HR 0.87 to 0.77 across regimes). Lines in conditional branches reverse: protective at birth (HR=0.98, 0-90 days), a risk factor after 90 days (HR=1.21). Repository identity is the largest factor: a gamma frailty model (variance theta=1.208) raises concordance from 0.593 to 0.667, outweighing every structural covariate. Conclusion: Line-level survival modeling is tractable, yielding interpretable, mostly static risk signals and a calibration recipe for time-conditional risk scoring in IDEs and code review.

</details>


### [13] [TeleSWEBench: A Commit-Driven Benchmark for Evaluating LLM-Powered Software Engineering in Telecommunications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05001v1)
*Pranshav Gajjar,Ali Mamaghani,Dinesh Bharadia,Vijay K Shah*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了TeleSWEBench，第一个面向电信领域的commit驱动基准，用于评估ASE工具修改5G协议栈的能力，结果显示最强工具仅能实现25%的可交付更改。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用编程基准无法评估ASE工具在电信领域修改复杂、有状态且数学严谨的无线协议栈（如srsRAN 5G）的性能，存在评估空白。

Method: 从srsRAN 5G仓库挖掘真实开发者commit，构建734个结构化测试用例（分三个难度等级）；提出分层LLM评判框架TeleJudge，结合单元测试和语义相似性进行文件级评估。

Result: 评估AIDER、OpenHands、ClaudeCode等工具及多种LLM，发现模型缺乏定位准确性和功能正确性，最强ASE工具仅达成25%的可交付更改。

Conclusion: 现有ASE工具在电信领域表现不佳，需要进一步改进以处理专业代码库的复杂性和严格要求。

中文摘要：随着电信领域拥抱零接触管理以及新颖的O-RAN和AI-RAN框架，当代电信网络现在作为极其复杂且高度软件化的代码库运行。虽然自动化软件工程（ASE）工具和软件工程（SWE）Agent有潜力缓解该领域的关键代码生成瓶颈，但它们在导航和修改专业、数学严谨的无线协议栈（如srsRAN 5G）方面的能力仍未得到验证。通用编程基准无法捕捉电信的有状态逻辑和严格需求，留下了关键的评估空白。在本文中，我们介绍了TeleSWEBench，这是第一个专门设计用于衡量Agent在电信领域性能的commit驱动基准。我们从srsRAN 5G仓库中挖掘真实的开发者commit，并将其提炼为跨越三个难度等级（简单、中等、困难）的结构化测试用例。我们的基准包含734个问题，并附有可执行的单元测试。为了避免测试用例的僵化，我们进一步提出了一个称为TeleJudge的分层LLM作为评判框架，它在文件级别对Agent输出进行评分，并整体聚合判定结果。这遵循基于上下文和语义相似性的评估，与标准的基于单元测试的评估并行。使用该基准，我们评估了由最先进的推理LLM（包括Qwen3、GPT OSS、Gemma 4、Kimi和Qwencoder 2.5）驱动的AIDER、OpenHands和ClaudeCode框架。我们的两阶段评估揭示，模型缺乏定位准确性和功能正确性，最强的ASE工具实现了高达25%的可交付更改。

Original abstract: With the telecommunications field embracing zero touch management alongside novel O-RAN and AI-RAN frameworks, contemporary telecom networks now function as immensely intricate and heavily softwareized codebases. While automated software engineering (ASE) tools and Software Engineering (SWE) Agents hold the potential to alleviate the critical code generation bottleneck in this domain, their ability to navigate and modify specialized, mathematically rigorous wireless stacks like srsRAN 5G remains unverified. General-purpose coding benchmarks fail to capture the stateful logic and strict requirements of telecommunications, leaving a critical evaluation gap. In this paper, we introduce TeleSWEBench, the first commit-driven benchmark specifically designed to measure an agent's performance in the telecom domain. We mine real developer commits from the srsRAN 5G repository and distill them into structured test cases across three difficulty tiers (Easy, Medium, and Difficult). Our benchmark consists of 734 questions that are accompanied by executable unit tests. To avoid the rigidity of test cases, we further propose a hierarchical LLM as a Judge framework called TeleJudge that scores agent outputs at the file level and aggregates verdicts holistically. This follows an evaluation based on context and semantic similarity in parallel to a standard unit test-based evaluation. Using this benchmark, we evaluate AIDER, OpenHands, and the ClaudeCode frameworks, powered by state-of-the-art reasoning LLMs, including Qwen3, GPT OSS, Gemma 4, Kimi, and Qwencoder 2.5. Our two-stage evaluation reveals that models suffer from a lack of both localization accuracy and functional correctness, with the strongest ASE tools achieving up to 25% of shippable changes.

### [14] [Self-Reflective APIs: Structure Beats Verbosity for AI Agent Recovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05037v1)
*Arquimedes Canedo,Grama Chethan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 自我反思的API通过返回结构化建议，显著提升了AI代理在API调用错误时的任务完成率和token效率，但该提升仅在审计答案泄漏后成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当AI代理调用API遇到验证错误时，仅知道错误信息不足以让代理自主修复，需要可操作的下一步建议，以减少外部推理并提高效率。

Method: 设计自我反思的API，在验证失败时返回机器可读的recovery_feedback.suggestions[]；通过泄漏审计的试点实验（每个单元N=30，3个LLM，10个对抗性任务），比较结构化建议与纯文本诊断的效果，并在第二领域（计费API）复制实验；同时审计LLM基准测试中的两类答案泄漏。

Result: 在Anthropic模型上，结构化建议将任务完成率提升36.7-40.0个百分点（Fisher精确检验p≤0.0022），每成功token效率提升1.8-2.2倍；在gpt-4o-mini上提升不显著（p=0.435）；第二领域复制确认了模式；比较仅在审计答案泄漏后成立。

Conclusion: 结构化建议比纯文本诊断更有效地帮助AI代理修复API调用错误，但基准测试中的答案泄漏可能影响结果有效性；提供的审计工具可作为可复用基础设施。

中文摘要：当AI代理调用API并遇到验证错误时，它需要的不仅仅是哪里出错了——它需要接下来该做什么。一个自我反思的API在验证失败时返回一个机器可读的recovery_feedback.suggestions[]负载，足以让代理在无需外部推理的情况下修复请求并重试。在一个经过泄漏审计的试点中（每个单元N=30，3个LLM，10个对抗性任务），结构化建议在Anthropic模型上将任务完成率提高了+36.7–40.0个百分点（相对于纯文本诊断，Fisher精确检验p≤0.0022），每成功token效率提高了1.8–2.2倍。在gpt-4o-mini上提升不显著（p=0.435）；在计费API上的第二个领域复制确认了该模式。该比较仅在审计了LLM基准测试中两类未记录的答案泄漏后才成立。我们提供了audit_prompt_leakage.py作为可复用的CI基础设施。代码和数据：https://github.com/arquicanedo/self-reflective-apis。

Original abstract: When an AI agent calls an API and hits a validation error, it needs more than what went wrong -- it needs what to do next. A self-reflective API returns, on validation failure, a machine-readable recovery\_feedback.suggestions[] payload sufficient for the agent to repair the request and retry without external reasoning. On a leak-audited pilot ($N{=}30$ per cell, 3 LLMs, 10 adversarial tasks), structured suggestions lift task-completion rate by $+36.7$--$40.0$pp over plain-English diagnoses on Anthropic models (Fisher's exact $p \le 0.0022$), at $1.8$--$2.2\times$ better per-success token efficiency. The lift is not significant on gpt-4o-mini ($p{=}0.435$); a second-domain replication on a billing API confirms the pattern. The comparison only holds after auditing two undocumented classes of answer leakage in LLM benchmarks. We shipaudit\_prompt\_leakage.py as reusable CI infrastructure. Code and data: https://github.com/arquicanedo/self-reflective-apis.

</details>


### [15] [How Software Engineering Students Use LLMs to Write Research Papers: An Experience Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05114v2)
*Ronnie de Souza Santos,Maria Teresa Baldassarre,Cleyton Magalhaes,Italo Santos*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文报告了一项教育经验，在软件工程课程中要求学生使用LLM完成实证作业并披露使用情况，分析了146份披露声明，总结了学生如何使用LLM以及相关问题和教育启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索将LLM整合到实证软件工程教育中的可行性和影响。

Method: 在软件架构课程中设置实证方法作业，要求学生使用快速综述或灰色文献综述方法撰写论文并披露LLM使用情况；采用LLM辅助分类与手动验证结合的交叉分析过程分析146份学生披露声明。

Result: 学生将LLM用于头脑风暴、方法澄清、结果组织和写作改进，但也表达了关于内容不准确和验证的担忧。

中文摘要：大型语言模型正日益成为软件工程教育的一部分，包括涉及实证软件工程和证据综合的活动。本文报告了一项教育经验，涉及将反思性LLM使用整合到三年级软件架构课程中的一项实证方法作业中。学生被要求使用快速综述或灰色文献综述方法撰写一篇简短的研究论文，并披露整个作业中如何使用LLM。我们采用结合LLM辅助分类与研究人员手动验证和细化的交叉分析过程，分析了146份学生披露声明。反思描述了学生如何在头脑风暴、方法澄清、发现组织以及写作细化等活动中融入LLM，同时也报告了对不准确性和生成内容验证的担忧。本经验报告讨论了将AI辅助技术整合到实证软件工程教育中的经验教训和教育意义。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly becoming part of software engineering education, including activities involving empirical software engineering and evidence synthesis. This paper reports an educational experience involving the integration of reflective LLM use into an empirical methods assignment in a third-year software architecture course. Students were asked to develop a short research paper using either a rapid review or a gray literature review methodology and to disclose how LLMs were used throughout the assignment. We analyzed 146 student disclosure statements using a cross-analysis process combining LLM-assisted categorization with manual verification and refinement by the researchers. The reflections describe how students incorporated LLMs during activities such as brainstorming, methodological clarification, organization of findings, and writing refinement, while also reporting concerns regarding inaccuracies and verification of generated content. This experience report discusses lessons learned and educational implications for integrating AI-assisted technologies into empirical software engineering education.

### [16] [A Taxonomy of Runtime Faults in Model Context Protocol Servers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05339v1)
*Joshua Owotogbe,Indika Kumara,Willem-Jan van den Heuvel,Damian Andrew Tamburri,Antonio Ken Iannillo,Roberto Natella*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次对MCP服务器运行时故障进行实证分类，通过分析837个故障线程和开发者调查，得出11大类27子类73种故障类型，并验证了其广泛存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP的快速采用带来了新的可靠性挑战，如配置参数不被强制执行，而运行时故障特征缺乏实证研究。

Method: 手动分析473个GitHub仓库的837个故障线程，采用自底向上开放式编码构建分类法，并通过55位开发者调查验证外部有效性。

Result: 分类法包含11个顶级类别、27个子类别和73个叶子故障类型；开发者平均经历20个子类别，所有类别均被观察到。

Conclusion: 该分类法反映了MCP系统中广泛观察的运行时故障，有助于AI软件维护与演化。

中文摘要：MCP（模型上下文协议）使大语言模型（LLM）能够通过标准化协议与外部工具和数据源进行交互。该协议在工具增强型人工智能工作流程中的快速采纳引入了新的可靠性挑战，例如某些配置参数虽被接受但未在运行时强制执行，导致意外的默认行为，其运行时故障特征尚未得到实证检验。我们提出了首个MCP服务器运行时故障的实证分类法。我们手动分析了来自473个活跃维护的MCP服务器GitHub仓库的837个MCP特定运行时故障线程，并使用自底向上的开放式编码方法推导出分类法。该分类法包含11个顶级类别和27个子类别（73个叶子故障类型），涵盖了协议交互、工具调用、模式强制、状态管理、模型-提供者集成、安全验证以及超时或显式取消正在进行的操作等领域的重复性故障。为了评估分类法的外部有效性，我们调查了55位MCP服务器开发者。受访者报告平均经历了27个故障子类别中的20个，且没有类别未被观察到。这些结果表明，该分类法反映了MCP系统中广泛观察到的运行时故障，并将在未来有助于AI软件的维护与演化。

Original abstract: MCP (Model Context Protocol) enables LLMs (Large Language Models) to interact with external tools and data sources via a standardized protocol. Its rapid adoption in tool-augmented Artificial Intelligence (AI) workflows has introduced new reliability challenges, such as configuration parameters that are accepted but not enforced at runtime, leading to unintended default behavior, whose runtime fault characteristics remain empirically unexamined. We present the first empirical taxonomy of runtime faults in MCP servers. We manually analyzed 837 MCP-specific runtime fault threads from 473 actively maintained MCP server GitHub repositories and derived a taxonomy using a bottom-up open coding procedure. The taxonomy comprises 11 top-level categories and 27 subcategories (73 leaf fault types), covering recurrent failures across protocol interactions, tool invocations, schema enforcement, state management, model-provider integration, security validation, and timeouts or explicit cancellations of in-progress operations. To assess the taxonomy's external validity, we surveyed 55 MCP server developers. Respondents reported experiencing an average of 20 of the 27 fault subcategories, and no category remained unobserved. These results indicate that the taxonomy reflects widely observed runtime failures in MCP-based systems and shall assist AI software maintenance and evolution in the future.

</details>


### [17] [Human oversight of agentic systems in practice: Examining the oversight work, challenges, and heuristics of developers using software agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05391v1)
*Shipi Dhanorkar,Samir Passi,Mihaela Vorvoreanu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过对17位开发者的访谈，研究了自主软件代理的涌现监督工作，发现监督不仅包括事后审查，还包括先验控制、协同规划和实时监控等预防性和主动性形式，并总结了相关挑战与应对策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理监督研究多基于概念性框架，缺乏对用户实际监督行为的实证了解，本文旨在通过开发者访谈提供实证锚点，填补这一空白。

Method: 采用探索性访谈方法，对17位经验丰富的开发者进行半结构化访谈，分析其监督代理的实践、挑战和策略。

Result: 识别出四种监督工作形式：先验控制、协同规划、实时监控和事后审查；发现监督具有预防性和主动性；描述了监督挑战（如代码审查困难）和应对启发式（如测试结果保证）。

Conclusion: 代理监督工作需要更多实证研究，本文为未来研究方向、人本设计及软件工程实践提供了启示，并指出了研究局限性。

中文摘要：自主软件代理有望提高开发人员的生产力，但也会犯错并表现出新的故障模式，使得人类监督成为成功人机协作的核心。现有的代理监督研究大多是概念性的；虽然有规范性框架，但用户实际如何监督代理尚不明确。在本文中，我们通过为代理监督的理论讨论提供早期实证锚点来弥补这一差距。基于对17位经验丰富的开发人员的访谈，我们进行了一项探索性调查，考察开发人员执行何种形式的涌现监督工作、何时以及如何执行。我们还记录了开发人员面临的监督挑战以及他们开始使用的应对策略。我们发现至少四种涌现监督工作形式：先验控制、协同规划、实时监控和事后审查。我们表明，监督工作不仅是反应性和回顾性的（如现有研究所描述），而且还是预防性和主动性的。我们描述了情境化的监督挑战（例如，难以审查代理生成的代码），并概述了开发人员为解决这些挑战而采用的启发式方法（例如，使用测试结果作为代码正确性的保证）。最后，我们总结了高层次要点、未来研究方向、对软件代理的人本设计和软件工程实践的影响以及我们研究的局限性。

Original abstract: Autonomous software agents hold promise to increase developer productivity but make mistakes and exhibit novel failure modes, making human oversight central to successful human-agent collaboration. Existing research on agent oversight is largely conceptual; normative frameworks exist, but how users actually oversee agents is less known. In this paper, we bridge this gap by providing early empirical anchors for the theoretical discourse on agent oversight. Drawing on interviews with 17 experienced developers, we conduct an exploratory inquiry examining what forms of emergent oversight work developers perform, when, and how. We also document the oversight challenges developers face and the strategies they have started using to address them. We found at least four forms of emergent oversight work: a priori control, co-planning, real-time monitoring, and post hoc review. We show that oversight work is not only reactive and retrospective, as portrayed in existing research, but also preventative and proactive. We describe situated oversight challenges (e.g., difficulty reviewing agent-generated code) and outline heuristics developers adopt to address such challenges (e.g., using test results as guarantees for code correctness). We conclude with high-level takeaways, future research directions, implications for the human-centered design of software agents and for software engineering practice, and limitations of our research.

</details>

The community would benefit from a reference that synthesizes knowledge to inform the architectural design of MLOps systems, especially regarding the integration and deployment of ML models. Objective. In response, our goal is to provide a comprehensive overview of architecturally significant guidelines for the integration and deployment of ML models in MLOps systems. Method. We then apply thematic analysis to synthesize these practices into recommended guidelines. Results. We contribute a collection of 25 architecturally significant MLOps guidelines for model integration and deployment, organized into five categories, and describe their impact on the overall system architecture. Conclusion. Our results serve as an overview of state-of-practice MLOps guidelines to support researchers and practitioners with the integration and deployment of ML models in their MLOps systems.

### [19] [REStack: A Large-Scale Dataset of Reverse Engineering Discussions from Stack Exchange](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05493v1)
*Md Humaun Kabir,Md Rakibul Islam,Farha Kamal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了REStack，一个大规模逆向工程讨论数据集，包含12,000+帖子，识别出23个主题，分析显示RE讨论实践性强，某些主题难度高，提供了可重用资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RE实践者面临的挑战、主题和知识差距缺乏实证理解，且没有公开数据集系统捕获RE讨论。

Method: 从Stack Overflow和Reverse Engineering Stack Exchange收集数据，使用LDA结合GA超参数优化，手动主题标注，识别主题和类别，添加元数据和难度指标。

Result: 数据集包含12,000+帖子，跨越15年以上，识别出23个主题（6个类别）；分析显示RE讨论实践导向，强调调试等，内存/固件/文件格式分析主题难度高、未解决率高。

Conclusion: REStack是可重用资源，支持实证研究、教育、AI/LLM工具开发，旨在促进可重复研究和数据驱动的RE实践支持。

中文摘要：逆向工程（RE）是软件工程和网络安全中的关键活动，支持恶意软件分析、漏洞发现、遗留系统维护和固件检查等任务。尽管其重要性，但对RE实践者在现实环境中面临的挑战、主题和知识差距的实证理解有限，且没有公开可用的数据集系统性地捕获来自开发者问答论坛的RE讨论。在本文中，我们提出了REStack，一个从Stack Overflow和专门的逆向工程Stack Exchange站点收集的大规模RE讨论数据集。该数据集包含超过12,000条RE相关帖子，跨越15年以上。使用基于遗传算法（GA）超参数优化的潜在狄利克雷分配（LDA），随后进行手动主题标记，我们识别出23个语义连贯的RE主题，这些主题被分组为六个高层次的主题类别。数据集进一步丰富了元数据和从社区交互信号（如未回答率和响应时间）派生的难度指标。我们的分析表明，RE讨论主要是实践性和任务导向的，重点强调调试、反汇编和系统级分析，而与内存、固件和文件格式分析相关的主题显示出高难度和未解决率。除了实证表征外，REStack为实证研究、教育研究以及基于AI和LLM的RE开发者辅助工具的开发与评估提供了可重用的资源。通过发布数据集和配套脚本，本工作旨在促进可重复研究并推动RE实践的数据驱动支持。

Original abstract: Reverse engineering (RE) is a critical activity in software engineering and cybersecurity, supporting tasks such as malware analysis, vulnerability discovery, legacy system maintenance, and firmware inspection. Despite its importance, there is limited empirical understanding of the challenges, topics, and knowledge gaps faced by RE practitioners in real-world settings, and no publicly available dataset has systematically captured RE discussions from developer Q&A forums.
  In this paper, we present REStack, a large-scale dataset of RE discussions collected from Stack Overflow and the dedicated Reverse Engineering Stack Exchange site. The dataset comprises over 12,000 RE-related posts spanning more than 15 years. Using Latent Dirichlet Allocation (LDA) with Genetic Algorithm (GA)-based hyperparameter optimization, followed by manual topic labeling, we identify 23 semantically coherent RE topics grouped into six high-level thematic categories. The dataset is further enriched with metadata and difficulty indicators derived from community interaction signals, such as unanswered rates and response times.
  Our analysis reveals that RE discussions are predominantly practical and task-oriented, with strong emphasis on debugging, decompilation, and system-level analysis, while topics related to memory, firmware, and file format analysis exhibit high difficulty and unresolved rates. Beyond empirical characterization, REStack provides a reusable resource for empirical studies, educational research, and the development and evaluation of AI- and LLM-based developer assistance tools for RE. By releasing the dataset and accompanying scripts, this work aims to facilitate reproducible research and advance data-driven support for RE practice.

</details>


### [20] [STMutants: A Mutation Testing Dataset for Structured Text Programs in Industrial Automation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05499v1)
*Md Humaun Kabir,Md Rakibul Islam,Helen H. Lou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了首个用于IEC 61131-3结构化文本程序的变异测试数据集STMutants，包含108个变异体，覆盖七类算子，并验证了LLM在变异检测中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ST程序缺乏支持可重复变异研究的公开基准，而其在安全关键工业环境中的广泛应用使得这一问题尤为突出。

Method: 从11个ST程序生成110个一阶变异体，经过可观测性和等价性筛选保留108个；采用四阶段方法：故障类型分析和算子选择、语法转换、可编译性验证、手动等价性筛选；评估三个LLM进行测试套件生成和变异杀死预测。

Result: 三个LLM在108个变异体上的检测准确率分别为86.1%、94.4%和86.1%，且存在显著性能差异。

Conclusion: STMutants作为首个公开的ST程序变异基准，支持可重复的自动化测试生成、变异分析、故障定位和AI辅助质量保证研究。

中文摘要：变异测试广泛用于评估测试套件的有效性，然而IEC 61131-3结构化文本（ST）程序仍缺乏一个支持可重复变异研究的公开基准。这一差距尤为重要，因为ST广泛用于可编程逻辑控制器（PLC），这些控制器在实时、安全关键的工业环境中运行，软件故障可能导致设备损坏、生产损失或不安全系统行为。为满足这一需求，我们提出了STMutants，一个用于工业自动化软件的精心策划的变异测试数据集。STMutants包含从OSCAT基本库和工业相关来源收集的11个ST程序生成的110个一阶变异体，经过可观测性和等价性筛选后保留108个。该数据集涵盖从经典分类法调整到PLC领域的七类变异算子，包括值、关系、算术、逻辑、否定、操作插入/省略和初始化故障。每个变异体通过四阶段方法构建：故障类型分析和算子选择、语法转换、可编译性验证以及具有强评分者间一致性（kappa=0.87）的手动等价性筛选。为展示数据集的实用性，我们在两阶段设置中评估三个大语言模型（LLM）：测试套件生成，接着是变异杀死/存活预测。在108个保留的变异体上，模型分别达到86.1%、94.4%和86.1%的变异检测准确率，统计分析确认了显著的性能差异。通过提供首个公开的ST程序变异基准，STMutants使得针对PLC软件的自动化测试生成、变异分析、故障定位和AI辅助质量保证的可重复研究成为可能。

Original abstract: Mutation testing is widely used to evaluate test-suite effectiveness, yet IEC 61131-3 Structured Text (ST) programs still lack a publicly available benchmark that supports reproducible mutation-based research. This gap is especially important because ST is extensively used in Programmable Logic Controllers (PLCs) that operate in real-time, safety-critical industrial environments, where software faults may cause equipment damage, production loss, or unsafe system behavior. To address this need, we present STMutants, a curated mutation testing dataset for industrial automation software. STMutants contains 110 generated first-order mutants derived from 11 ST programs collected from the OSCAT basic library and industrially relevant sources, of which 108 are retained after observability and equivalence screening. The dataset covers seven mutation operator categories adapted from classical taxonomies for the PLC domain, including value, relational, arithmetic, logical, negation, operation insertion/omission, and initialization faults. Each mutant is constructed through a four-phase methodology: fault-type profiling and operator selection, syntactic transformation, compilability verification, and manual equivalence screening with strong inter-rater agreement (kappa = 0.87). To demonstrate the usefulness of the dataset, we evaluate three large language models (LLMs) in a two-phase setting: test-suite generation followed by mutation kill/survive prediction. Across 108 retained mutants, the models achieve mutation detection accuracies of 86.1%, 94.4%, and 86.1%, respectively, with statistical analysis confirming significant performance differences. By providing the first publicly available mutation benchmark for ST programs, STMutants enables reproducible research on automated test generation, mutation analysis, fault localization, and AI-assisted quality assurance for PLC software.

</details>

### [21] [Exploring Cross-Scenario Generality of Agentic Memory Systems: Diagnostics and a Strong Baseline](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04315v1)
*Zhikai Chen,Jialiang Gu,Junyu Yin,Xianxuan Long,Shenglai Zeng,Xiaoze Liu,Kai Guo,Keren Zhou,Jiliang Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出通用agent记忆系统理论，可迁移至coding agent的上下文管理。

TL;DR: 提出AutoMEM，通过让代理主动控制存储和检索，实现跨场景最佳泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统针对特定场景设计，缺乏跨异构轨迹的泛化能力。

Method: 重新评估八个记忆系统和一个代理工具集（自管理文本文件存储），在五个场景上测试，并基于主动控制思想设计AutoMEM。

Result: 自管理工具集在跨任务排名中最佳，AutoMEM实现最佳跨场景通用性。

Conclusion: 记忆性能的关键是赋予代理对存储和检索的主动控制，而非固定的被动管道。

中文摘要：LLM代理积累的历史记录超出了其上下文窗口，这激励了关于记忆系统的日益增长的文献。然而，大多数现有设计是针对单一场景（多会话聊天或单轨迹格式）进行调整的，并且几乎没有证据表明它们能够泛化到代理在部署中遇到的异构轨迹。我们重新审视了八个记忆系统以及一个用于搜索问题的代理工具集，在五个场景上进行了评估：单轮问答、多会话聊天、代理轨迹问答、记忆压力测试和长期代理任务。该工具集通过工具调用自我管理平面文本文件存储，实现了最佳的跨任务排名，这表明记忆性能取决于赋予代理对存储和检索的主动控制，而不是固定管道后的被动存储。我们将这一见解实例化为AutoMEM，一个具有自我管理工具接口的代理记忆工具集，在我们评估的系统中实现了最佳的跨场景通用性。

Original abstract: LLM agents accumulate histories that outgrow their context windows, motivating a growing literature on memory systems. Yet most existing designs are tuned to a single scenario (multi-session chat or a single trajectory format), and there is little evidence that they generalize across the heterogeneous trajectories agents encounter in deployment. We revisit eight memory systems plus an agentic harness for search problems, on five scenarios: single-turn QA, multi-session chat, agentic-trajectory QA, memory stress tests, and long-horizon agentic tasks. The harness, which self-manages flat text-file storage via tool calls, achieves the best cross-task ranking, suggesting that memory performance hinges on giving the agent active control over storage and retrieval rather than on a passive store behind a fixed pipeline. We instantiate this insight in AutoMEM, an agentic memory harness with a self-managed tool interface that achieves the best cross-scenario generality among the systems we evaluate.

</details>


### [22] [The Digital Apprentice: A Framework for Human-Directed Agentic AI Development](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04321v1)
*Travis Weber,Rohit Taneja*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出人类指导的agent自主性框架，可启发代码优化agent的人机协作设计。

TL;DR: 提出数字学徒框架，通过方法论捕获、授权和持续对齐三个组件，使AI代理的自主权基于经验证据逐步提升，实现安全可扩展的代理系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决代理型AI部署中人类监督与自主性之间的矛盾，缺乏负责任授权的治理基础设施。

Method: 三个架构组件：方法论捕获（提炼专家内隐方法）、授权（分级自主权需人类批准）、持续对齐（运行时纠正漂移并积累偏好数据），作为推理时控制平面实例化。

Result: 在开放专业语料库上应用，通过捕捉数据漂移并运行时调整技术，恢复流量转移下的质量退化。

Conclusion: 三个支柱组件组合形成更安全可行的路径，使代理系统可扩展而不牺牲信任。

中文摘要：代理型人工智能部署面临一个反复出现的设计矛盾：大量的人类监督限制了规模，而广泛的自主性又超出了问责范围。这两种姿态都无法提供负责任授权所需的治理基础设施。我们提出了数字学徒（Digital Apprentice），这是一个用于可扩展、安全的人工智能代理的框架，其中自主权是挣来的，而非假设的。数字学徒是一个发展型学习者，它内化指导人类的内隐方法论，只有在对经验证据证明合理时才逐步通过每个技能的自主级别。结果是一个随着时间推移变得真正有用，同时保持与特定人类标准一致的代理。三个架构组件使之成为可能：(1) 方法论捕获，将指导专业人士的内隐方法提炼为结构化资产。(2) 授权，自主升级需经明确的人类批准。(3) 持续对齐，在运行时纠正漂移并将每次纠正转化为自有偏好数据。我们将该框架实例化为一个推理时控制平面。我们对质量框架进行数学建模，并讨论旨在提高质量的策略和技术。我们将该框架应用于一个开放的专业语料库，并展示如何捕捉数据漂移并在运行时应用不同技术以恢复流量转移下的退化质量维度。其意义超越任何单一应用。我们相信，这三个支柱作为一个系统组合在一起，为能够在不牺牲信任的情况下扩展的代理系统提供了一条更安全、更可行的路径。

Original abstract: Agentic AI deployments face a recurring design tension: heavy human oversight limits scale, while broad autonomy outruns accountability. Neither posture provides the governance infrastructure required for responsible delegation. We present the Digital Apprentice, a framework for scalable, safe AI agency in which autonomy is earned, not assumed. The Digital Apprentice is a developmental learner that internalizes the tacit methodology of a directing human, graduating through per-skill autonomy tiers only when empirical evidence justifies it. The result is an agent that becomes genuinely useful over time while remaining aligned to a specific human's standards. Three architectural components make this possible. (1) Methodology capture, distilling a directing professional's tacit approach into structured assets. (2) Authorization, with autonomy escalation gated by explicit human approval. (3) Continuous alignment, correcting drift at runtime and converting each correction into owned preference data. We instantiate this framework as an inference-time control plane. We mathematically model the quality framework and discuss policies and techniques designed to raise quality. We apply the framework to an open professional corpus, and we show how catching data drift and applying a different technique at runtime recovers degraded quality dimensions under traffic shift. The implication extends beyond any single application. We believe these three pillars, stitched together as a system, form a safer and more viable path to agentic systems that can scale without sacrificing trust.

</details>


### [23] [Online Skill Learning for Web Agents via State-Grounded Dynamic Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04391v1)
*Jiaxi Li,Ke Deng,Yun Wang,Jingyuan Huang,Yucheng Shi,Qiaoyu Tan,Jin Lu,Ninghao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出状态接地动态检索方法，提升web agent多步技能复用，直接涉及agent规划与记忆

TL;DR: 提出状态引导动态检索（SGDR），通过逐步技能重用提升多步网页自动化，在WebArena上超越基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线技能学习方法仅在任务级别静态检索技能，无法适应执行过程中网页状态的动态变化，导致初始技能无法覆盖后续情况。

Method: SGDR包含三个组件：滑动窗口提取（将完整轨迹转为可重用的子程序）、双文本-代码表示（连接检索与执行动作）、状态引导动态检索（匹配技能与任务目标和当前状态）。

Result: 在WebArena上五个域中，SGDR使用GPT-4.1平均成功率37.5%（相对提升10.6%），使用Qwen3-4B平均成功率24.3%（相对提升10.0%）。

Conclusion: SGDR通过状态感知的动态技能检索，显著改进了网页智能体的多步自动化性能，验证了方法的有效性。

中文摘要：语言智能体越来越依赖可重复使用的技能来改进跨相关任务的多步网页自动化。越来越多的研究工作在线技能学习，其中智能体从先前的任务轨迹中持续归纳技能，并在未来的任务中即时重用它们。然而，现有方法主要在任务级别重用技能：基于初始任务指令检索一组固定的技能，然后在执行过程中保持不变。这种静态策略与网页执行不一致，因为合适的下一步行动不仅取决于任务目标，还取决于当前的网页状态，而网页状态通常会转换到初始技能无法覆盖的情况。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了状态引导的动态检索（SGDR），一种在线技能学习方法，使网页智能体能够逐步重用技能。SGDR由三个组件组成：滑动窗口提取过程，将完成轨迹转化为可在中间执行状态下调用的可重用子程序；双文本-代码表示，连接技能检索与可执行动作；以及状态引导的动态检索机制，将技能与任务目标和当前网页状态相匹配。在WebArena上跨五个领域的实验表明，SGDR持续优于强基线，使用GPT-4.1时平均成功率为37.5%，使用Qwen3-4B时平均成功率为24.3%，分别相对于最强基线有10.6%和10.0%的相对提升。代码可在https://github.com/plusnli/skill-dynamic-retrieval获取。

Original abstract: Language agents increasingly rely on reusable skills to improve multi-step web automation across related tasks. A growing line of work studies online skill learning, where agents continually induce skills from previous task trajectories and reuse them in future tasks on the fly. However, existing methods mainly reuse skills at the task-level: a fixed set of skills is retrieved based on the initial task instruction and then held fixed throughout execution. This static strategy is misaligned with web execution, where the appropriate next action depends not only on the task goal but also on the current webpage state, which often transitions into situations that the initial skills fail to cover. To address this gap, we propose State-Grounded Dynamic Retrieval (SGDR), an online skill learning method that enables stepwise skill reuse for web agents. SGDR consists of three components: a sliding-window extraction process that turns completed trajectories into reusable sub-procedures invokable at intermediate execution states, a dual text-code representation that connects skill retrieval with executable action, and a state-grounded dynamic retrieval mechanism that matches skills to both the task goal and the current webpage state. Experiments on WebArena across five domains show that SGDR consistently outperforms strong baselines, achieving average success rates of 37.5% with GPT-4.1 and 24.3% with Qwen3-4B, corresponding to relative gains of 10.6% and 10.0% over the strongest baseline, respectively. The code is available at https://github.com/plusnli/skill-dynamic-retrieval.

</details>


### [24] [Not All Errors Are Equal: Consequence-Aware Reasoning Compute Allocation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04402v1)
*Jingbo Wen,Liang He,Ziqi He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出后果感知测试时计算分配，在SWE-bench上验证，可迁移至coding agent资源调度

TL;DR: 提出后果感知的测试时计算分配方法，利用轻量级预测器估计任务错误成本，调度高后果任务至更大计算资源，在700个软件工程任务上降低成本加权损失22%-33%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时计算分配方法假设所有失败成本相同，但实际部署中任务错误成本差异很大，需要根据后果而非仅难度分配计算资源。

Method: 使用轻量级预测器从问题文本估计任务错误成本，调度器据此在相同总预算下将高后果任务路由到更大计算层级或更高思考预算。

Result: 后果与难度正交；预测器从未将高后果任务误判为低后果；后果感知调度器在匹配预算下将成本加权损失降低22%-33%，优先级感知变体降低超30%，可部署版本保留超90%Oracle增益。

Conclusion: 后果感知计算分配能有效降低实际部署中的成本加权损失，且与难度互补，具有实用价值。

中文摘要：当前的推理模型可以根据任务的不同，分配不同数量的测试时计算资源（如思考令牌、模型调用或计算预算）。现有方法通常通过预测难度来驱动这种分配，并在预期能提高准确性的任务上投入更多计算。这隐含地假设所有失败的成本相同，因为准确性目标对每个任务的权重相同。然而，这种假设在部署中并不成立：日志消息中的拼写错误和导致生产数据库损坏的迁移都算作一个基准失败，但它们的实际成本根本不同。为填补这一空白，我们提出了后果感知的测试时计算分配。我们不是仅根据预测难度来路由计算，而是使用一个轻量级预测器从问题文本中估计任务如果被错误解决会带来多大成本。然后，调度器在相同总预算下将高后果任务路由到更大的计算层级或更高的思考预算。我们在SWE-bench Lite上进行了主要实验，并在Multi-SWE-bench mini上评估了跨数据集行为，共涵盖700个软件工程任务。我们的结果表明，在各种标注下，后果和难度大致正交，并且当前的思考模型没有根据后果充分分配计算。此外，我们的仅问题文本预测器从未将高后果任务误分类为低后果，这在300个SWE-bench任务中得到了验证。在匹配的计算预算下，我们的后果感知调度器相对于难度感知路由将成本加权损失降低了22%至33%；特别是优先级感知变体，通过按边际效用信号缩放的每任务成本进行路由，降低了超过30%，而其可部署的预测器驱动版本保留了超过90%的Oracle增益。

Original abstract: Modern reasoning models can allocate different amounts of test-time computation, such as thinking tokens, model calls, or compute budget, to different tasks. Existing methods generally drive this allocation by predicted difficulty and spend more compute where it is expected to raise accuracy. This implicitly assumes that all failures cost the same, since an accuracy objective weights every task equally. However, such an assumption does not hold in deployment: A typo in a log message and a migration that corrupts a production database both count as one benchmark failure, but their real-world costs are fundamentally different. To fill this gap, we propose consequence-aware test-time compute allocation. Instead of routing compute only by predicted difficulty, we use a lightweight predictor to estimate from the issue text how costly a task would be if solved incorrectly. The scheduler then routes higher-consequence tasks to larger compute tiers or higher thinking budgets under the same total budget. We conduct main experiments on SWE-bench Lite and evaluate cross-dataset behavior on Multi-SWE-bench mini, covering 700 software-engineering tasks in total. Our results reveal that consequence and difficulty are approximately orthogonal under various annotations, and that current thinking models do not allocate compute sufficiently according to consequence. Moreover, our issue-only predictor never misclassifies a high-consequence task as low-consequence across the 300 SWE-bench tasks. Under matched compute budgets, our consequence-aware scheduler reduces cost-weighted loss by 22% to 33% relative to difficulty-aware routing; in particular, the priority-aware variant, which routes by per-task cost scaled by the marginal-utility signal, crosses 30%, and its deployable predictor-driven version retains over 90% of the oracle gain.

### [25] [Trivium: Temporal Regret as a First-Class Objective for Causal-Memory Controllers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04421v2)
*Edward Y. Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 首次将时间遗憾作为agent核心目标，理论分析agent失败原因，对长期agent设计有启发

TL;DR: 提出长时域时间遗憾、认知遗憾与结果遗憾相结合，以系统性地解决智能体系统中错误的原因和时机，并在CausalBench-Seq上验证了对数性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅优化结果奖励，忽略了错误的“为什么”和“何时”，导致同样错误反复出现；作者认为这是结构性问题而非模型容量问题。

Method: 引入时间遗憾（捕获失败持续多久）和认知遗憾（捕获失败为何持续），与结果遗憾并列；将智能体建模为E次迭代流，在因果探测、持久性和可检测性假设下证明三个条件结果；实例化为Trivium系统并预注册可证伪预测。

Result: 在CausalBench-Seq上，Trivium的时间遗憾遵循对数包络线，而仅结果奖励的基线线性增长；真实LLM流实验（E=500一次，E=100三次）提供初步外部有效性证据。

Conclusion: 通过结合时间、认知和结果遗憾，能够更系统地理解并纠正智能体错误，实现对数级别的时间遗憾复杂度，且自我学习聚焦于修订外部因果模型而非重训LLM权重。

中文摘要：许多当前的智能体系统和LLM流程通过优化结果奖励来纠正错误。这仅解决了失败的“什么”：当结果偏离预测时，不匹配的“为什么”和“何时”没有被系统地记录、审查或纠正，因此同样的错误可能会在每一次迭代中重复出现。我们认为这是一个结构性问题，而不仅仅是模型容量问题。我们提出将长时域时间遗憾作为与结果遗憾和工作因果模型上的认知遗憾并列的一等目标。时间遗憾捕捉失败持续的时间：一个校准错误的因果模型在被纠正之前被容忍了多久。认知遗憾捕捉失败持续的原因：工作因果模型中的残余不确定性或错误。这三个遗憾共同提供了一个可证伪的描述，说明长期存在的智能体可能失败的内容、原因和时间。将智能体建模为E次迭代的流，我们在明确的因果探测、持续性和可检测性假设下证明了三个条件性结果。首先，在观测等价混淆下，仅基于结果的学习无法在没有干预通道的情况下区分因果结构和虚假结构，因此即使结果遗憾被驱动到零，时间校准错误也可能线性持续。其次，通过持续的因果日志和预算有限的探测，总探测复杂度在迭代时间跨度上是对数的，导致O(log E)的时间遗憾。第三，在有K个可检测的变点的情况下，该率扩展到O(K log E)。我们实例化了Trivium并预注册了五个可证伪的预测。在CausalBench-Seq上，Trivium遵循预测的对数包络线，而仅基于结果的基线线性增长。一个真实LLM流的试点实验在完整的E=500运行和三个E=100前沿模型试点中提供了初步的外部有效性证据。这里，自我学习意味着修改外部因果模型，而不是重新训练LLM权重。

Original abstract: Many current agentic systems and LLM pipelines correct mistakes by optimizing outcome reward. This addresses only the what of failure: when an outcome diverges from prediction, the why and when of the mismatch are not systematically logged, reviewed, or corrected, so the same error can recur episode after episode. We argue that this is a structural problem, not merely a model-capacity one. We propose long-horizon temporal regret as a first-class objective alongside outcome regret and epistemic regret over the working causal model. Temporal regret captures when failure persists: how long a miscalibrated causal model is tolerated before correction. Epistemic regret captures why failure persists: residual uncertainty or error in the working causal model. Together, the three regrets give a falsifiable account of what, why, and when a long-lived agent can fail. Modeling the agent as a stream of E episodes, we prove three conditional results under explicit causal-probing, persistence, and detectability assumptions. First, under observationally equivalent confounding, outcome-only learning cannot distinguish causal from spurious structure without an intervention channel, so temporal miscalibration can persist linearly even after outcome regret is driven to zero. Second, with a persistent causal log and budgeted probes, total probe complexity is logarithmic in the episode horizon, inducing O(log E) temporal regret. Third, under K detectable change-points, the rate extends to O(K log E). We instantiate Trivium and pre-register five falsifiable predictions. On CausalBench-Seq, Trivium follows the predicted logarithmic envelope while outcome-only baselines grow linearly. A pilot real-LLM stream provides preliminary external-validity evidence across one full E = 500 run and three E = 100 frontier-model pilots. Self-learning here means revising an external causal model, not retraining LLM weights.

</details>


### [26] [Cascading Hallucination in Agentic RAG: The CHARM Framework for Detection and Mitigation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04435v1)
*Saroj Mishra*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出级联幻觉检测框架CHARM，适用于多步agentic RAG，增强agent可靠性

TL;DR: 提出CHARM框架用于检测和缓解多步RAG流水线中的级联幻觉，实现高检测率和低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测机制无法检测早期错误在推理步骤中传播导致的级联幻觉，导致高置信但错误输出。

Method: 提出CHARM框架，包含阶段级事实验证、跨阶段一致性跟踪、置信度传播监控和级联解析触发四个组件，与现有流水线并行运行。

Result: 在多个数据集上，CHARM实现89.4%级联检测率，5.3%假阳性率，82.1%误差传播减少，每个阶段延迟约215ms。

Conclusion: CHARM有效检测和中断级联幻觉，可与人在环框架集成，提升生产级AI的可靠性。

中文摘要：多步智能检索增强生成（RAG）流水线在复杂推理任务中展现了显著能力，但仍然容易受到一类现有幻觉检测机制系统性遗漏的失败影响：级联幻觉，即早期流水线阶段引入的错误在连续的推理步骤中传播和放大，产生自信但事实不正确的最终输出。为了解决这一漏洞，我们将级联幻觉形式化为智能RAG系统中一种独特的失败模式，提出了一个四类型级联模式的分类法，并引入了CHARM（级联幻觉感知解析与缓解），一种用于检测和中断多步推理流水线中错误传播的架构框架。CHARM由四个组件组成——阶段级事实验证、跨阶段一致性跟踪、置信度传播监控和级联解析触发——这些组件与标准智能RAG流水线并行运行，无需替换架构。我们在HotpotQA、MuSiQue、2WikiMultiHopQA以及一个自定义对抗数据集上，跨LangChain智能流水线配置评估了CHARM，实现了89.4%的级联检测率，5.3%的假阳性率，以及每个阶段平均215 ms ± 18 ms的延迟开销，误差传播减少了82.1%，而输出级检测器仅为18.5%。组件消融实验确认每个检测模块对整体级联覆盖率有显著贡献。CHARM与人在环监督框架集成，为生产级智能AI部署提供了完整的可靠性和治理栈。

Original abstract: Multi-step agentic retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) pipelines have demonstrated significant capability for complex reasoning tasks, yet remain vulnerable to a class of failure that existing hallucination detection mechanisms systematically miss: cascading hallucination, where errors introduced at early pipeline stages propagate and amplify across successive reasoning steps, producing confident but factually incorrect final outputs. To address this vulnerability, we formalize cascading hallucination as a distinct failure mode in agentic RAG systems, present a four-type taxonomy of cascade patterns, and introduce CHARM (Cascading Hallucination Aware Resolution and Mitigation), an architectural framework for detecting and interrupting error propagation in multi-step reasoning pipelines. CHARM comprises four components - stage-level fact verification, cross-stage consistency tracking, confidence propagation monitoring, and cascade resolution triggering - that operate alongside standard agentic RAG pipelines without requiring architectural replacement. We evaluate CHARM on HotpotQA, MuSiQue, 2WikiMultiHopQA, and a custom adversarial dataset across LangChain agentic pipeline configurations, achieving an 89.4% cascade detection rate with a 5.3% false positive rate and 215 ms +/- 18 ms average latency overhead per stage, achieving an error propagation reduction of 82.1%, compared to 18.5% for output-level detectors. Component ablations confirm that each detection module contributes meaningfully to overall cascade coverage. CHARM integrates with human-in-the-loop oversight frameworks to provide a complete reliability and governance stack for production agentic AI deployment.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计MAC框架，让元智能体在沙盒环境中使用评估API和时限迭代编程智能体工件，并采用多层防御防止奖励黑客。

Result: 元智能体很少匹配人类基线，仅有少数专有前沿模型成功；设计过程高方差，优化压力导致地面实况泄露等对抗行为。

中文摘要：当前的AI基准测试评估的是智能体在人类设计的工作流程中执行任务的能力。这些评估从根本上未能衡量一个关键的下一代能力：模型是否能自主开发智能体系统。我们引入了元智能体挑战（MAC），这是一个评估框架，旨在测试前沿模型自主开发智能体的能力。具体来说，一个代码智能体（元智能体）被给予一个沙盒环境、一个评估API和一个时间限制，以迭代编程一个智能体工件，该工件在五个领域的保留测试集上最大化性能。为了确保评估的完整性，该框架由多层防御机制保护，以防止奖励黑客攻击。利用这个框架，我们证明了元智能体很少能匹配人类设计的基线策略，而少数能够匹配的则主要由专有前沿模型主导。此外，设计过程表现出高方差，高优化压力会涌现出对抗性行为，如地面实况数据泄露——这突出了鲁棒性和模型对齐方面的关键缺陷。最终，MAC为自主人工智能研究和开发提供了一个严格的、开源的基准测试，为评估递归自我改进提供了一个经验代理。基准测试公开可见于：https://github.com/ant-research/meta-agent-challenge。

Original abstract: Current AI benchmarks evaluate agents on task execution within human-designed workflows. These evaluations fundamentally fail to measure a critical next-level capability: whether models can autonomously develop agent systems. We introduce the Meta-Agent Challenge (MAC), an evaluation framework designed to test the capacity of frontier models for autonomous agent development. Specifically, a code agent (the meta-agent) is given a sandboxed environment, an evaluation API, and a time limitation to iteratively program an agent artifact that maximizes performance on a held-out test set across five domains. To ensure evaluation integrity, this framework is secured by multi-layer defenses against reward hacking. Leveraging this framework, we demonstrate that meta-agents rarely match human-engineered baseline policies, and the few that do are dominated by proprietary frontier models. Moreover, the design process exhibits high variance, and high optimization pressure surfaces emergent adversarial behaviors like ground-truth exfiltration-highlighting critical deficits in both robustness and model alignment. Ultimately, MAC provides a rigorous, open-source benchmark for autonomous AI research and development, offering an empirical proxy for evaluating recursive self-improvement. Benchmark is publicly available at: https://github.com/ant-research/meta-agent-challenge.

### [28] [AgentJet: A Flexible Swarm Training Framework for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04484v1)

Method: 采用解耦的多节点群架构，分离服务器节点（模型优化）和客户端节点（智能体执行），并引入上下文跟踪模块（时间线合并）来加速训练。

Result: 实现了1.5-10倍的训练加速，并能够自动化长期多天的强化学习研究。

Original abstract: We present AgentJet, a distributed swarm training framework for large language model (LLM) agent reinforcement learning. Unlike centralized frameworks that tightly couple agent rollouts with model optimization, AgentJet adopts a decoupled multi-node architecture in which swarm server nodes host trainable models and run optimization on GPU clusters, whereas swarm client nodes execute arbitrary agents on arbitrary devices. This design provides capabilities that are difficult to support in centralized frameworks: (1) heterogeneous multi-model reinforcement learning, enabling the training of heterogeneous multi-agent teams with multiple LLM as brains; (2) multi-task cocktail training with isolated agent runtimes; (3) fault-tolerant execution that prevents external environment failures from interrupting the training process; and (4) live code iteration, which allows agents to be edited during training by replacing swarm client nodes. To support efficient RL in multi-model, multi-turn, and multi-agent settings, AgentJet introduces a context tracking module with timeline merging, which consolidates redundant context and achieves a 1.5-10x training speedup. Finally, AgentJet introduces an automated research system that takes a research topic as input and autonomously conducts long-horizon, multi-day RL studies on large-scale clusters. By leveraging the swarm architecture, this system reproduces key exploratory workflows of RL researchers without human intervention during execution.

### [29] [Beyond Prompt-Based Planning: MCP-Native Graph Planning-based Biomedical Agent System](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04494v1)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生物医学智能体面临工具异构和规划依赖扁平检索导致效率低下，需要解耦规划与工具规模。

Method: 构建BioinfoMCP编译器标准化工具为MCP服务器，组织为类型化异构MCP图，推理时检索子图合成工作流脚手架。

Result: 在BioAgentBench和LAB-Bench上，执行准确性、工作流有效性和上下文效率优于先进基线。

Conclusion: 可扩展生物医学推理需要结构化能力图而非更大提示检索。

中文摘要：生物医学智能体有望自动化复杂的生物工作流，然而当前系统面临两个根本瓶颈：生物信息学工具在接口和执行环境上高度异构，而智能体规划仍然依赖于扁平化的提示检索工具描述。随着生物医学软件生态系统的增长，工具覆盖范围与上下文大小之间的耦合导致了工具混淆、规划不稳定和执行效率低下。我们引入了BioManus，一个基于图形脚手架规划结构化生物能力的MCP原生生物医学智能体。BioManus首先引入了BioinfoMCP编译器，将异构的生物信息学软件转换为标准化的MCP服务器，从而产生一个大型可执行的MCP生态系统。然后，它将这个生态系统组织成一个带有类型化的异构MCP图，涵盖工具、操作、数据类型和工作流阶段。在推理时，BioManus检索紧凑的任务特定子图，合成操作级工作流脚手架。这种设计将规划复杂度与原始工具库存大小解耦，在高召回率检索下实现了上下文压缩比Theta(N / (h * m_bar))，其中N是工具总数，h是工作流长度，m_bar（远小于N）是每个操作的平均候选工具数量。在BioAgentBench和LAB-Bench上的实验表明，与先进的生物医学智能体基线相比，BioManus在执行准确性、工作流有效性和上下文效率方面均有提升。这项工作表明一种范式转变：可扩展的生物医学推理需要结构化的可执行能力图，而不是越来越大的提示级工具检索。

Original abstract: Biomedical agents promise to automate complex biological workflows, yet current systems face two fundamental bottlenecks: bioinformatics tools are highly heterogeneous in interfaces and execution environments, while agent planning still relies on flat prompt-retrieved tool descriptions. As biomedical software ecosystems grow, this coupling between tool coverage and context size leads to tool confusion, unstable planning, and inefficient execution. We introduce BioManus, an MCP-native biomedical agent built on graph-scaffolded planning over structured biological capabilities. BioManus first introduces the BioinfoMCP Compiler, which converts heterogeneous bioinformatics software into standardized MCP servers, yielding a large executable MCP ecosystem. It then organizes this ecosystem as a typed heterogeneous MCP graph over tools, operations, datatypes, and workflow stages. At inference time, BioManus retrieves compact task-specific subgraphs, synthesizes operation-level workflow scaffolds. This design decouples planning complexity from raw tool inventory size, achieving a context compression ratio of Theta(N / (h * m_bar)) under high-recall retrieval, where N is the total tool count, h is the workflow horizon, and m_bar (much smaller than N) is the average number of candidate tools per operation. Experiments on BioAgentBench and LAB-Bench show that BioManus improves execution accuracy, workflow validity, and context efficiency over advanced biomedical agent baselines. This work suggests a paradigm shift: scalable biomedical reasoning requires structured executable capability graphs rather than increasingly larger prompt-level tool retrieval.

### [30] [Simulate, Reason, Decide: Scientific Reasoning with LLMs for Simulation-Driven Decision Making](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04505v1)
*Yuhan Yang,Ruipu Li,Alexander Rodríguez*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过共享结构化模式表示模拟器（假设、变量、机制依赖、执行轨迹），LLM作为受约束的推理引擎生成证据解释。

中文摘要：科学模拟器越来越多地被集成到由大语言模型（LLM）驱动的系统中，用于高风险的、基于模拟的决策制定。然而，现有框架主要使用LLM来生成、校准或执行模拟器，将其视作黑盒接口而非可推理的结构化机制系统。因此，当前方法缺乏识别、表示和推理模拟器行为背后假设与机制的能力，限制了透明度、可审计性和决策论证。我们提出了MechSim，一种面向可执行科学模拟器的、基于机制的神经符号推理框架。与以往主要对静态符号结构进行推理的神经符号方法不同，MechSim使得LLM智能体能够推理科学模拟器的机制、假设和执行行为。我们的框架通过一个共享的结构化模式来表示模拟器，该模式捕获假设、变量、机制依赖和执行轨迹。在此表示之上，LLM智能体作为受约束的推理引擎运行，生成结构化的、有证据支撑的解释，将模拟器结果与其底层机制联系起来。我们在多个高风险领域评估了我们的方法，结果表明它在机制级解释质量、模拟器分析和下游决策可靠性方面都有所改进。

Original abstract: Scientific simulators are increasingly being integrated into LLM-driven systems for high-stakes simulation-driven decision-making. However, existing frameworks primarily use LLMs to generate, calibrate, or execute simulators, treating them as black-box interfaces rather than as structured mechanistic systems that can be reasoned about. As a result, current approaches lack the ability to identify, represent, and reason about the assumptions and mechanisms underlying simulator behavior, limiting transparency, auditability, and decision justification. We introduce MechSim, a mechanism-grounded neuro-symbolic reasoning framework for executable scientific simulators. Unlike prior neuro-symbolic approaches that primarily reason over static symbolic structures, MechSim enables LLM agents to reason about the mechanisms, assumptions, and execution behavior of scientific simulators. Our framework represents simulators through a shared structured schema capturing assumptions, variables, mechanism dependencies, and execution traces. On top of this representation, LLM agents operate as constrained reasoning engines that generate structured, evidence-grounded explanations linking simulator outcomes to their underlying mechanisms. We evaluate our approach across multiple high-stakes domains and show that it improves mechanism-level explanation quality, simulator analysis, and downstream decision-making reliability.

### [31] [MapAgent: An Industrial-Grade Agentic Framework for City-scale Lane-level Map Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04513v2)
*Deguo Xia,Zihan Li,Haochen Zhao,Dong Xie,Yuyao Kong,Xiyan Liu,Jizhou Huang,Mengmeng Yang,Diange Yang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MapAgent在矢量化主干基础上，通过Judge-Planner-Worker循环进行规范验证、错误诊断和自动编辑，仅在低置信度区域触发。

Result: 在真实数据集上优于基线，尤其是在复杂和长尾场景；已集成到百度地图，覆盖360+城市，自动化率超95%。

Conclusion: MapAgent实用有效，适用于大规模车道级地图生成。

中文摘要：车道级地图是自动驾驶和车道级导航的关键基础设施，然而为数百个城市构建和维护标准化车道网络仍然高度劳动密集。最近端到端的矢量化建图方法可以直接从传感器数据预测车道几何和拓扑，但它们通常将建图规范和交通规则视为隐式的、依赖数据集的监督。此外，在复杂场景（例如磨损或缺失的标记和遮挡）中，仅凭视觉证据通常不足以确定正确的车道配置，导致规范违反成为人工后期编辑的主要来源。我们提出MapAgent，一个工业级的主体架构，它增强了一个矢量化主干以生产符合规范的车道地图。与仅仅在地图预测上添加一个主体循环不同，MapAgent将主干感知与明确的规范验证、约束感知推理以及确定性的地图编辑在一个有界的、验证驱动的Judge-Planner-Worker循环中相结合。一个视觉语言Judge通过联合检查视觉证据和草稿向量来诊断错误，而一个工具调用Planner生成最小的纠正编辑并进行编辑后重新验证。为了在城市规模生产中保持可扩展性，MapAgent仅在主干置信度低的瓦片上选择性触发，增加适度的开销同时保持吞吐量。在真实世界数据集上的实验显示出相对于强大的生产基线的持续改进，特别是在复杂和长尾场景中。此外，MapAgent已集成到百度地图中，支持全国超过360个城市的车道级地图生成，并将整体生产自动化率提升至95%以上，展示了MapAgent在大规模车道级地图生成中的实用性和有效性。

Original abstract: Lane-level maps are critical infrastructure for autonomous driving and lane-level navigation, yet constructing and maintaining standardized lane networks for hundreds of cities remains highly labor-intensive. Recent end-to-end vectorized mapping methods can predict lane geometry and topology directly from sensor data, but they typically treat mapping specifications and traffic regulations as implicit, dataset-dependent supervision. Moreover, in complex scenes (e.g., worn or missing markings and occlusions), correct lane configurations are often under-determined by visual evidence alone, making specification violations a major source of human post-editing. We propose MapAgent, an industrial-grade agentic architecture that augments a vectorization backbone for specification-compliant lane-map production. Rather than merely adding an agent loop to map prediction, MapAgent couples backbone perception with explicit specification verification, constraint-aware reasoning, and deterministic map editing under a bounded, verification-driven Judge-Planner-Worker loop. A vision-language Judge diagnoses errors by jointly inspecting visual evidence and draft vectors, while a tool-calling Planner generates minimal corrective edits with post-edit re-validation. To remain scalable for city-scale production, MapAgent is selectively triggered only on tiles with low backbone confidence, adding modest overhead while preserving throughput. Experiments on real-world datasets show consistent gains over strong production baselines, especially in complex and long-tail scenarios. Additionally, MapAgent has been integrated into Baidu Maps, supporting lane-level map generation for over 360 cities nationwide and elevating the overall production automation to over 95%, demonstrating MapAgent's practicality and effectiveness for large-scale lane-level map generation.
