### [96] [Personal AI Agent for Camera Roll VQA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05275v1)
*Thao Nguyen,Krishna Kumar Singh,Donghyun Kim,Yong Jae Lee,Yuheng Li*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 个人相册VQA agent，具有分层记忆和工具使用，一般agent设计可借鉴

TL;DR: 提出了camroll数据集和camroll-agent，用于个人相机胶卷视觉问答，实验证明其优于现有方法，并揭示了个性化视觉记忆与文本记忆的不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI助手缺乏对长期、高度个性化的视觉内容流的理解能力，无法高效导航大规模个人相机胶卷并回答相关问题。

Method: 收集50个用户的31,476张图像和2,500个手工标注的QA对，设计配备分层记忆和工具集的camroll-agent。

Result: camroll-agent在多个基线和方法中表现出更优的性能。

Conclusion: 个性化视觉记忆需要不同于标准文本记忆的方法，尤其是处理一致性、视觉细节和用户特定上下文时。

中文摘要：我们研究个人相机胶卷视觉问答场景。在该场景中，对话式AI助手可以访问用户的个人相机胶卷并检索相关照片来回答查询，从简单的事实性问题（例如“我昨天尝试的食物的名称？”）到更开放的问题（例如“推荐一些我从未吃过的菜品”）。鉴于个人相机胶卷的巨大规模（即多年、数百到数千张照片），一个成功的AI助手需要理解长期、高度个性化的视觉内容流，以便导航和定位正确和/或相关信息。为支持这一点，我们收集并手动标注了模拟真实世界使用场景的问题。最终数据集camroll包含50个用户、31,476张图像和2,500个问答对。我们进一步设计了camroll-agent，一个配备分层记忆和最少工具集的对话式AI智能体，用于高效导航大规模个性化视觉记忆。实验结果表明，camroll-agent在长上下文理解AI智能体系统中优于众多基线和方法。总之，camroll数据集和camroll-agent凸显了AI智能体长上下文推理中的差距：个性化视觉记忆需要不同于标准长上下文文本记忆的方法，特别是在一致性、视觉细节和用户特定上下文存在的情况下。

Original abstract: We study the personal camera roll visual question answering setting. In this setting, a conversational AI assistant can access a user's personal camera roll and retrieve relevant photos to answer queries, ranging from simple factual questions (e.g., ``Name of the food I tried yesterday?'') to more open-ended ones (e.g., ``Recommend some dishes I have never eaten before''). Given the vast nature of the personal camera roll (i.e., multiple years, hundreds to thousands of photos), a successful AI assistant needs to understand a long-horizon, highly personalized visual content stream in order to navigate and locate the correct and/or relevant information. To support this, we collect and manually annotate questions that mimic real-world usage. The final dataset, camroll, contains 50 users, 31,476 images, and 2,500 QA pairs. We further design camroll-agent, a conversational AI agent equipped with hierarchical memory and a minimal set of tools for efficient navigation over large, personalized visual memory. Experimental results show that camroll-agent outperforms numerous baselines and methods for long-context understanding AI agents system. Together, the camroll dataset and camroll-agent highlight the gap in AI agents' long-context reasoning: personalized visual memory requires different approaches from standard long-context textual memory, especially when consistency, visual details, and user-specific context are present.

</details>

### [97] [Towards Multi-Agent-Simulation-Based Community Note Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18268v1)
*Changxi Wen,Shuning Zhang,Bohao Chu,Yuwei Chuai,Hui Wang,Dai Shi,Xin Yi,Hewu Li*

Main category: cs.SI

Selection reason: 多agent仿真评估框架，可迁移至多agent代码审查或协作优化场景。

TL;DR: 提出MultiCom框架，通过角色引导的多智能体评分和聚合算法，在社区事实核查中优于其他方法，平均准确率84.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决社区事实核查中交叉共识评级延迟和低比例的问题。

Method: 创建ComRate数据集，提出MultiCom框架，包括基于矩阵分解的评分者聚类、角色智能体生成结构化评估，以及折外校准聚合算法。

Result: MultiCom在评估集上平均准确率84.7%，平衡准确率68.3%，宏F1 60.1%。

Conclusion: MultiCom有效提高了社区事实核查评级的可靠性和效率。

中文摘要：基于交叉共识的社区事实核查正在社交媒体平台上迅速扩展。然而，由人类贡献者评级的交叉共识社区事实核查的延迟和低比例仍然是一个重大挑战。为了解决这个问题，我们首先创建了ComRate，一个大规模数据集，包含来自𝕏的250万条社区笔记和超过2.09亿条评分。然后我们提出了MultiCom，一个用于社区笔记评估的角色引导多智能体评分框架。MultiCom通过在矩阵分解的评分者空间中聚类贡献者并提示角色智能体根据官方社区笔记评分模式生成结构化评估，来模拟多样化的评分者群体。这些智能体输出结构化和可解释的判断，例如置信度、一致性信号和理由。一种折外校准的聚合算法结合了原始投票和诊断性理由信号等特征，以实现可靠的预测。广泛评估表明，MultiCom优于其他方法，在评估集上达到了84.7%的平均准确率（平衡准确率68.3%，宏F1 60.1%）。

Original abstract: Community-based fact-checking that relies on cross-consensus is expanding rapidly on social media platforms. However, the delay and low-ratio of cross-consensus community fact-checks rated by human contributors remains a significant challenge. To address this, we first created ComRate, a large-scale dataset comprising 2.5 million community notes and over 209 million ratings sourced from $\mathbb{X}$. We then propose MultiCom, a persona-guided multi-agent rating framework for community note evaluation. MultiCom simulates diverse rater population by clustering contributors in a matrix-factorized rater space and prompting persona agents to generate structured assessments based on the official community notes rating schema. These agents output structured and explainable judgments, such as confidence, agreement signals and reasons. An out-of-fold calibrated aggregation algorithm combines features such as raw votes and diagnostic reason signals for reliable prediction. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that MultiCom outperforms alternative methods, achieving an average accuracy of 84.7% (balanced accuracy 68.3%, macro-F1 60.1%) on the evaluation set.

</details>

### [98] [Latent Anchor-Driven Test Generation for Deep Neural Networks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04310v1)
*Bin Duan,Matthew B. Dwyer,Guowei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Latte是一个基于潜在空间的黑盒测试框架，通过种子中心一步潜在突变生成语义邻近、多样且能揭示故障的测试用例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DNN测试方法在探索可控性、故障多样性和语义漂移之间存在权衡，难以同时兼顾。

Method: Latte使用预训练VQ-VAE编码种子，从替代类别采样锚点定义方向进行一步潜在突变，然后量化解码回输入空间。

Result: 在5个数据集和10个模型上，Latte在相同预算下提高了故障暴露和多样性，并保持了低种子相对语义漂移。

Conclusion: Latte有效生成了高质量的测试用例，提升了DNN测试的效率和效果。

中文摘要：深度神经网络（DNN）越来越多地被部署在安全关键和安全敏感的应用中，这使得严格的测试对于识别和缓解模型弱点至关重要。现有的DNN测试方法要么探索输入空间，要么探索学习到的潜在空间。虽然潜在空间生成比直接输入空间突变能更好地保持合理性，但当前方法仍然面临探索可控性、故障多样性和种子相对语义漂移之间的权衡。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了Latte，一个黑盒测试框架，通过利用潜在空间生成语义邻近、多样且能揭示故障的测试用例。具体来说，Latte使用预训练的VQ-VAE对每个输入种子进行编码，并沿从替代类别采样的锚点定义的方向执行以种子为中心的一步潜在突变，然后进行量化和解码回到输入空间。这探索了每个种子在学习到的潜在流形上的局部邻域，从而在相同预算下产生更多数量和更广泛多样性的触发预测差异的测试用例。我们在5个数据集和10个DNN模型上评估了Latte，包括单模型和多模型测试场景。在评估的数据集和模型上，Latte在匹配的测试预算下提高了故障暴露和多样性。在单模型设置中，它还保持了相对于源种子的低种子相对语义漂移。

Original abstract: Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) are increasingly being deployed in security-critical and safety-sensitive applications, which makes rigorous testing essential to identify and mitigate model weaknesses. Existing DNN testing approaches explore either the input space or a learned latent space. While latent-space generation can better maintain plausibility than direct input-space mutation, current methods still face a trade-off among exploration controllability, failure diversity, and seed-relative semantic drift. To overcome these limitations, we propose Latte, a black-box testing framework that generates semantically proximate, diverse, and fault-revealing test cases by leveraging the latent space. Specifically, Latte encodes each input seed with a pre-trained VQ-VAE and performs a seed-centered, one-step latent mutation along directions defined by anchors sampled from alternative classes, followed by quantization and decoding back to the input space. This explores local neighborhoods around each seed within the learned latent manifold, resulting in a larger number and broader diversity of oracle-triggering prediction discrepancies under the same budget. We evaluated Latte on 5 datasets and 10 DNN models in single-model and multi-model testing scenarios. Across the evaluated datasets and models, Latte improves fault exposure and behavioral diversity under matched testing budgets. Under the single-model setting, it also maintains low seed-relative semantic drift with respect to the source seeds.

</details>


### [99] [Testing Neural Networks via Bayesian-Guided Exploration of Decision Landscapes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04314v1)
*Bin Duan,Meiru Che,Guowei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BayesWarp通过可解释显著性识别关键区域并利用不确定性感知的贝叶斯优化引导变异，在保持数据分布与语义邻近的同时高效发现多样化故障，提升了测试有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出BayesWarp，使用可解释显著性技术识别决策关键输入区域进行变异，并采用不确定性感知的贝叶斯优化自适应引导测试过程。

中文摘要：随着神经网络越来越多地部署在安全关键领域，测试对于评估和提高其可靠性至关重要。现有的测试方法，无论是黑盒还是白盒，主要使用全局变异或覆盖引导策略，这两种方法都难以在保持与原始数据分布和语义邻近的同时，高效地发现多样化的模型故障。我们提出了BayesWarp，一个测试框架，通过可解释的显著性技术识别决策关键的输入区域并进行变异，并使用不确定性感知的贝叶斯优化策略自适应地引导测试过程，从而在保持与原始数据的分布和语义邻近的同时，发现多样化的故障。在MNIST、CIFAR-10和ImageNet上对六个神经网络模型的评估表明，BayesWarp在固定的变异预算下提高了故障发现、故障多样性、测试用例质量和关键神经元覆盖率。这些结果表明BayesWarp提高了测试有效性。此外，使用生成的故障用例进行微调可以改善模型性能。

Original abstract: As neural networks are increasingly deployed in safety-critical domains, testing is essential to evaluate and improve their reliability. Existing testing methods, whether black-box or white-box, primarily use global mutation or coverage-guided strategies, both of which struggle to efficiently uncover diverse model failures while remaining proximate to the original data distribution and semantics. We propose BayesWarp, a testing framework that addresses this limitation by mutating decision-critical input regions identified via interpretable saliency techniques and adaptively guiding the testing process using an uncertainty-aware Bayesian Optimization strategy, enabling the discovery of diverse failures while preserving distributional and semantic proximity to the original data. Evaluation on MNIST, CIFAR-10, and ImageNet across six neural network models shows that BayesWarp improves failure discovery, failure diversity, test case quality, and critical neuron coverage under a fixed mutation budget. These results demonstrate that BayesWarp improves testing effectiveness. Moreover, fine-tuning with the generated failure cases leads to improvements in model performance.

### [100] [TD-Grokking: Learning from Zero-Reward Problems by Training-Time Decomposition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09883v1)
*Ningyuan Xi,Hao Xu,Hongsheng Xin,Ning Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 训练时分解零奖励问题，方法可应用于agent分解复杂任务，属于通用训练改进。

TL;DR: 提出TD-Grokking框架，通过训练时将零奖励问题递归分解为可验证子问题，提供有效训练信号，提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR在零奖励问题上无法提供优化信号，先前方法受限于任务约束或不完全。

Method: 训练时分解框架，递归分解问题为子问题，形成层次树，叶子节点可给出非零奖励。

Result: 在数学和医学任务上优于GRPO和基线方法，将零奖励转化为可用信号，性能一致提升。

Conclusion: 训练时分解有效解决了零奖励问题，实现了性能提升。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在推理任务上取得了显著进展，这主要归功于后训练范式，尤其是带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）。然而，一个关键瓶颈仍然存在：RLVR在高度具有挑战性的零奖励问题上失败，因为所有采样的推理轨迹都产生统一的失败结果，无法提供优化信号来驱动模型改进。先前解决这一限制的努力，如密集过程监督、部分奖励分配或前缀引导探索，受限于固有的任务约束，或者未能完全装备策略模型以解决原始棘手问题所必需的能力。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了TD-Grokking，一种针对零奖励问题的训练时分解框架。它递归地将棘手根问题分解为自包含、可验证的子问题，形成层次树，其中可解决的叶子节点提供非零奖励。在数学和医学任务上的评估表明，TD-Grokking优于vanilla GRPO以及所有基线方法。结合详细分析，这些结果证实了训练时分解有效地将零奖励示例转化为可用的训练信号，从而实现一致的性能提升。我们的代码和数据集可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TD-Grokking-6567/获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made remarkable progress in reasoning tasks, largely driven by post-training paradigms, especially reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). However, a critical bottleneck persists: RLVR fails on highly challenging zero-reward problems, where all sampled reasoning trajectories yield uniformly failed outcomes, providing no optimization signal to drive model improvement. Prior efforts to address this limitation, such as dense process supervision, partial reward assignment, or prefix-guided exploration, suffer from inherent task constraints or do not fully equip the policy model with the capabilities necessary to solve the original intractable problems. To address this, we propose TD-Grokking, a training-time decomposition framework for zero-reward problems. It recursively decomposes intractable root problems into self-contained, verifiable subproblems, forming hierarchical trees where solvable leaves provide non-zero rewards. Evaluations on mathematical and medical tasks show that TD-Grokking outperforms vanilla GRPO as well as all baseline approaches. Together with detailed analysis, these results confirm that training-time decomposition effectively converts zero-reward examples into usable training signals, enabling consistent performance gains. Our code and datasets are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TD-Grokking-6567/.

</details>


### [101] [SocraticPO: Policy Optimization via Interactive Guidance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09887v1)
*Zirui Liu,Jie Ouyang,Qi Liu,Xianquan Wang,Jiayu Liu,Tingyue Pan,Qingchuan Li,Jing Sha,Zhenya Huang,Shijin Wang,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于教师引导的policy优化，可改进agent在线学习策略

TL;DR: SocraticPO通过引入教师提供的苏格拉底式自然语言指导和奖励衰减机制，改进了强化学习在大型语言模型推理中的性能，减少了捷径学习和策略脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL方法使用标量奖励监督推理，缺乏对模型错误修正的解释，导致捷径学习和脆弱策略。

Method: 提出SocraticPO框架，在RL轨迹中引入教师诊断和纠正性文本指导，并对教师干预后的正确回答施加奖励衰减。

Result: 在SciKnowEval科学推理基准上，SocraticPO优于强RL和自蒸馏基线，消融实验证明指导和奖励衰减均必不可少。

Conclusion: 通过文本指导和奖励衰减，SocraticPO可有效提升策略鲁棒性并减少对辅助纠正的依赖，且易于集成到现有策略梯度方法中。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）在大型语言模型中通常使用标量结果奖励（如二元正确性）来监督推理。这种奖励提供了优化方向，但很少解释模型应如何修正其错误推理，这可能会鼓励捷径学习和脆弱的策略。我们提出SocraticPO（苏格拉底式策略优化），一个策略优化框架，通过苏格拉底式的自然语言指导来增强RL的轨迹。在轨迹生成过程中，学生首先独立回答；如果答案不正确，教师诊断该尝试并提供简洁的纠正性指导，之后学生在扩展的上下文下继续。关键的是，这种指导与奖励衰减配对：在教师干预后获得的正确答案仅获得衰减的奖励，防止策略将教师帮助视为获取奖励的免费路径。由于SocraticPO仅修改轨迹生成过程而保持标准期望奖励目标不变，它可以插入到现有的策略梯度后端（如Reinforce++）中。此外，由于教师仅提供文本级别的指导，SocraticPO可以利用更强的黑盒教师模型，而无需访问logits或分布匹配。在SciKnowEval的本科水平科学推理基准上，SocraticPO优于强RL和自蒸馏基线。消融实验表明，针对性的指导和奖励衰减都是必要的，其中奖励衰减减轻了对辅助纠正的依赖。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models usually supervises reasoning with scalar outcome rewards, such as binary correctness. Such rewards provide an optimization direction but rarely explain how a model should revise its mistaken reasoning, which can encourage shortcut learning and brittle policies. We propose \textbf{SocraticPO} (Socratic Policy Optimization), a policy-optimization framework that augments RL rollouts with Socratic-style natural-language guidance. During rollout, the student first answers independently; if the answer is incorrect, a teacher diagnoses the attempt and provides concise corrective guidance, after which the student continues under the expanded context. Crucially, this guidance is paired with reward decay: correct answers obtained after teacher intervention only receive decayed rewards, preventing the policy from treating teacher help as a free path to reward. Since SocraticPO only modifies the rollout process while leaving the standard expected-reward objective intact, it can be plugged into existing policy-gradient backends such as Reinforce++. Moreover, because the teacher provides only text-level guidance, SocraticPO can leverage stronger black-box teacher models without requiring access to logits or distribution matching. On undergraduate-level scientific reasoning benchmarks from SciKnowEval, SocraticPO improves over strong RL and self-distillation baselines. Ablations show that both targeted guidance and reward decay are necessary, with reward decay mitigating reliance on assisted correction.

### [102] [Trace-Mediated Peak Bias: Bridging Temporal Credit Assignment and Cognitive Heuristics in Deep Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04735v1)
*Viktor Veselý,Aleksandar Todorov,Erwan Escudie,Matthia Sabatelli*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 深度RL中时间信用分配问题，对agent训练有潜在启发

TL;DR: 发现深度强化学习中的痕迹介导峰值偏差（TMPB），解释了峰终定律的机制，并表明自适应优化器可缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间信用分配与非线性函数逼近的相互作用未被充分理解，且深度强化学习中存在系统性失效模式。

Method: 通过分析深度强化学习中的资格迹机制，识别出TMPB，并理论推导其成因。

Result: TMPB导致智能体偏好峰值奖励而非累积回报，原因是痕迹放大远端TD误差造成梯度冲击，固定步长SGD无法归一化；自适应优化器可缓解。

Conclusion: 类人显著性扭曲可能自然产生于分布式系统中信用分配的数学约束，自适应优化是合理价值估计的理论必要条件。

中文摘要：时间信用分配是生物和人工智能的核心，但其与非线性函数逼近的相互作用尚未被充分理解。我们识别出深度强化学习中的一种系统性失效模式，称为痕迹介导的峰值偏差（TMPB）。在中等资格迹深度下，智能体非理性地偏好具有高幅度奖励'峰值'的轨迹，而非具有更高累积回报的替代轨迹。这为峰终定律提供了机制性解释：峰终定律是一种人类记忆偏差，其中体验根据其最强烈的时刻而非综合效用进行判断。我们表明，TMPB的出现是因为痕迹将远端时间差分误差放大为'梯度冲击'，固定步长的随机梯度下降无法归一化这些冲击，导致全局高估。相反，自适应优化器通过二阶矩归一化减轻了这种病态。我们的结果表明，类人显著性扭曲可能自然产生于分布式系统中信用分配的数学约束，并且自适应优化是合理价值估计的理论必要条件。

Original abstract: Temporal credit assignment is central to both biological and artificial intelligence, yet its interaction with non-linear function approximation is poorly understood. We identify a systematic failure mode in deep reinforcement learning (RL) termed Trace-Mediated Peak Bias (TMPB). At intermediate eligibility trace depths, agents irrationally prefer trajectories with high-magnitude reward ``peaks'' over alternatives with higher cumulative returns. This provides a mechanistic account of the Peak-End Rule: a human memory bias where experiences are judged by their most intense moments rather than integrated utility. We show that TMPB emerges because traces amplify distal Temporal Difference errors into ``gradient shocks'' that fixed-step-size Stochastic Gradient Descent cannot normalize, leading to global overestimation. Conversely, adaptive optimizers mitigate this pathology via second-moment normalization. Our results suggest that human-like saliency distortions may emerge naturally from the mathematical constraints of credit assignment in distributed systems, and that adaptive optimization is a theoretical necessity for rational value estimation.

</details>


### [103] [Activation Steering of Video Generation Models via Reduced-Order Linear Optimal Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04775v1)
*Jihoon Hong,Alice Chan,Qiyue Dai,Julian Skifstad,Glen Chou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 视频生成模型激活控制，最优控制方法可迁移

TL;DR: 提出LA-LQR，一种基于最优控制的降阶激活引导框架，用于减少T2V模型的不良生成同时保持质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有T2V引导方法粗糙、非前瞻，导致过度引导和内容退化。

Method: 将T2V推理视为动态系统，通过投影到低维潜在空间、估计局部线性动力学、求解LQR问题获得引导信号。

Result: 在概念引导和视频安全基准上减少不安全生成，保持提示保真度和视觉质量。

Conclusion: LA-LQR有效实现最小侵入性引导，且理论保证。

中文摘要：文本到视频（T2V）模型在大规模网络数据上训练后可能生成不良内容，这促使人们采取干预措施来减少有害输出，同时不牺牲视觉质量。激活引导提供了一种有吸引力的机制替代微调和提示过滤，但现有的T2V引导方法仍然有限，通常采用粗糙、非前瞻性的干预，可能导致过度引导和内容退化。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了潜在激活线性二次型调节器（LA-LQR），一种用于最小侵入性T2V引导的降阶最优控制框架。LA-LQR将T2V推理公式化为一个动态系统，并计算闭环反馈干预，将激活引导至期望的特征设定点，同时惩罚不必要的扰动。为了使最优控制对高维视频激活可行，我们将激活投影到从对比提示对导出的低维、任务相关子空间，估计该潜在空间中的局部线性动力学，并求解潜在LQR问题以获取特定时间步和层的引导信号。我们提供了将潜在设定点跟踪与原始激活空间特征控制相联系的理论界，并实证验证了降阶潜在动力学的保真度。在概念引导和视频安全基准测试中，LA-LQR相对于基线减少了不安全生成，同时保持了提示保真度和视觉质量。

Original abstract: Text-to-video (T2V) models trained on large-scale web data can generate undesired content, motivating interventions that reduce harmful outputs without sacrificing visual quality. Activation steering offers an attractive mechanistic alternative to finetuning and prompt filtering, but existing T2V steering methods remain limited, typically applying coarse, non-anticipative interventions that can lead to oversteering and content degradation. To close this gap, we propose Latent Activation Linear-Quadratic Regulator (LA-LQR), a reduced-order optimal control framework for minimally invasive T2V steering. LA-LQR formulates T2V inference as a dynamical system and computes closed-loop feedback interventions that steer activations toward desired feature setpoints while penalizing unnecessary perturbations. To make optimal control feasible for high-dimensional video activations, we project activations onto a low-dimensional, task-relevant subspace derived from contrastive prompt pairs, estimate local linear dynamics in this latent space, and solve a latent LQR problem to obtain timestep- and layer-specific steering signals. We provide theoretical bounds relating latent setpoint tracking to raw activation-space feature control, and empirically validate the fidelity of the reduced latent dynamics. On concept steering and video safety benchmarks, LA-LQR reduces unsafe generations relative to baselines, while preserving prompt fidelity and visual quality.

### [104] [Learning While Acting: A Skill-Enhanced Test-Time Co-Evolution Framework for Online Lifelong Learning Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04815v2)
*Bo Mao,Jie Zhou,Yutao Yang,Xin Li,Xian Wei,Qin Chen,Xingjiao Wu,Liang He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在LifelongAgentBench上平均性能提升7个绝对百分点。

Conclusion: LifeSkill有效提升LLM智能体在线终身学习能力。

中文摘要：终身学习对于在动态、交互环境中运行的大型语言模型（LLM）智能体至关重要。然而，现有的用于长周期任务的终身学习智能体通常依赖离散技能或过去经验检索，在推理时使用静态参数，这阻碍了它们像人类学习者一样持续内化测试时的反馈。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出了技能增强的测试时协同进化（LifeSkill），这是一个面向在线终身学习智能体的两阶段强化学习框架。具体来说，我们设计了验证器引导的技能学习，通过根据多个技能条件策略滚动的平均验证器成功率对候选技能进行奖励，解决了技能提取缺乏直接监督的问题，鼓励模型生成对解决任务有用的技能，而不仅仅是文本上合理的技能。此外，我们引入了在线技能内化，通过将技能条件轨迹转化为奖励信号，在测试时交互过程中持续改进策略模型。这使得智能体能够直接将推理能力内化到其参数中，避免了经验检索的上下文膨胀。在LifelongAgentBench上的实验表明，与现有的终身学习智能体基线相比，LifeSkill将平均性能提高了7个绝对百分点。

Original abstract: Lifelong learning is essential for Large Language Model (LLM) agents operating in dynamic, interactive environments. However, existing lifelong learning agents for long-horizon tasks typically depend on discrete skill or past experiences retrieval with static parameters during inference, which prevents them from continuously internalizing test-time feedback like human learners. To bridge this gap, we propose Skill-enhanced Test-Time Co-Evolution (\texttt{LifeSkill}), a two-stage reinforcement learning framework for Online Lifelong Learning Agents. Specifically, we design Verifier-Guided Skill Learning that addresses the lack of direct supervision for skill extraction by rewarding candidate skills according to the average verifier success of multiple skill-conditioned policy rollouts, encouraging the model to generate skills that are useful for solving tasks rather than merely plausible in text. Furthermore, we introduce Online Skill Internalization, which continuously improves the policy model during test-time interaction by transforming skill-conditioned trajectories into reward signals. This enables the agent to directly internalize reasoning capabilities into its parameters, avoiding the context bloat of experience retrieval. Experiments on LifelongAgentBench show that LifeSkill improves average performance by 7 absolute points by comparing with existing lifelong agent baselines.

### [105] [PreAct-Bench: Benchmarking Predictive Monitoring in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09890v1)
*Hainiu Xu,Italo Luis da Silva,Jiangnan Ye,Yuhao Wang,Wei Liu,Linyi Yang,Jonathan Richard Schwarz,Nicola Paoletti,Yulan He,Hanqi Yan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出LLM agent轨迹安全预测基准，属于agent安全评测与可迁移方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全研究是回顾性的，只能事后检测伤害，需要前瞻性的风险预测。

Method: 定义预测性监测任务，构建PreActBench基准（1,000对道德/不道德轨迹，5个领域），使用Prefix Foresight F1指标评估LLM、安全护栏和潜在探测方法在不同轨迹比例下的性能。

Result: 人类表现较好，但即使强大模型在预测监测上仍具挑战。

Conclusion: 预测性监测对LLM安全重要但困难，需未来导向的风险推理。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被部署为能够朝着给定目标执行多步动作轨迹的自主智能体。虽然现有的安全研究侧重于从完整轨迹中检测不道德行为，但这种范式从根本上来说是回顾性的：它仅在伤害已经发生后识别伤害。在这项工作中，我们研究了一个关键但被忽视的安全任务，我们称之为预测性监测：仅给定部分动作轨迹，模型能否推断出它是否会在大动作执行之前达到不道德的行为？为了支持这一任务，我们提出了PreActBench，一个包含跨越五个领域的1,000个配对道德和不道德动作轨迹的基准。我们使用我们的前缀远见F1指标，评估了各种LLM、安全护栏模型和潜在探测方法在不同部分动作轨迹比例下的表现。结果显示，虽然人类取得了有希望的性能，但即使对于强大的模型，预测性监测仍然具有挑战性，凸显了LLM安全中对面向未来的风险推理的需求。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of executing multi-step action trajectories toward a given objective. While existing safety research has focused on detecting unethical behavior from complete trajectories, this paradigm is fundamentally retrospective: it identifies harm only after it has already occurred. In this work, we study a critical yet overlooked safety task, which we term Predictive Monitoring: given only a partial action trajectory, can a model infer whether it will culminate in an unethical action before the overt action is executed? To support this task, we present PreActBench, a benchmark of 1,000 paired ethical and unethical action trajectories spanning five domains. We evaluate a range of LLMs, safety guardrail models, and latent probing methods across varying fractions of the action trajectory using our Prefix Foresight F1 metric. Results show that while humans achieve promising performance, predictive monitoring remains challenging even for strong models, highlighting the need for future-oriented risk reasoning in LLM safety.

### [106] [Reproducing, Analyzing, and Detecting Reward Hacking in Rubric-Based Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04923v1)
*Xuekang Wang,Zhuoyuan Hao,Shuo Hou,Hao Peng,Juanzi Li,Xiaozhi Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基于评分的强化学习中，策略模型可能利用裁判模型的潜在偏见导致奖励破解，但现实中的破解行为微妙且与多种偏见纠缠，难以研究。

中文摘要：基于评分的强化学习（Rubric-based RL）使用大型语言模型作为裁判（LaaJ）根据评分标准对模型输出进行评分作为奖励。然而，策略模型可能会利用裁判中的潜在偏见，导致奖励破解和无效或不安全的训练结果。在现实世界的基于评分的强化学习中，这种破解行为往往很微妙，并与多种裁判偏见交织在一起，使其难以分析、检测和缓解。在本文中，我们引入了CHERRL，一个用于基于评分的强化学习的可控破解环境。通过向LaaJ注入已知偏见，CHERRL能够稳定地再现奖励破解，明确观察奖励发散，并精确识别破解开始。这为研究基于评分的强化学习中奖励破解的机制和缓解措施提供了一个干净的实验测试平台。为了展示其实用性，我们从可发现性和可利用性的角度分析了不同的裁判偏见，并探索了一种基于代理的系统，用于从训练日志中自动检测奖励破解的开始。代码和环境公开在https://github.com/THUAIS-Lab/CHERRL。

Original abstract: Rubric-based reinforcement learning (RL) uses an LLM-as-a-Judge (LaaJ) to score model outputs according to rubrics as rewards. However, policy models may exploit latent biases in the judge, leading to reward hacking and ineffective or unsafe training outcomes. In real-world rubric-based RL, such hacking behaviors are often subtle and entangled with multiple judge biases, making them difficult to analyze, detect, and mitigate. In this paper, we introduce CHERRL, a controllable hacking environment for rubric-based RL. By injecting known biases into LaaJ, CHERRL enables stable reproduction of reward hacking, explicit observation of reward divergence, and precise identification of hacking onset. This provides a clean experimental testbed for studying the mechanisms and mitigations of reward hacking in rubric-based RL. To demonstrate its utility, we analyze different judge biases from the perspectives of discoverability and exploitability, and explore an agent-based system for automatically detecting reward hacking onset from training logs. The code and environment are publicly available at https://github.com/THUAIS-Lab/CHERRL.

### [107] [Policy-Conditioned Counterfactual Credit for Verifiable Reinforcement Learning of Long-Horizon Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05263v1)
*Renwei Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL用于长程语言agent，含反事实信贷和验证奖励，可迁移

TL;DR: 提出CVT-RL，通过干预有效性门控和反事实贡献估计，在多个长程任务上提升成功率并减少黑客行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在长程语言智能体中存在学习不支持证据链、信念漂移和捷径动作的问题，过程奖励仅具相关性而无法估计因果贡献。

Method: 提出CVT-RL算法，包含约束策略梯度、密集可验证奖励、干预有效性门控和策略条件反事实贡献（PCCC）估计器；通过删除、语义替换、证据替换和工具输出扰动定义干预，使用冻结参考策略采样续写，并采用选择调整的双重稳健估计器增强优势；增广拉格朗日约束非支持声明、跳过验证、工具篡改和不安全调用。

Result: 在长上下文QA、ALFWorld、ScienceWorld及网页/工具任务上，CVT-RL将平均成功率从基线75.4%提升至78.9%，证据F1从78.9提升至82.8，黑客行为从7.2%降至3.9%；人类审计黑客行为为4.6%，统计显著（p<0.01）。

Conclusion: 谨慎范围的反事实信用与有效性门控、诊断和可验证约束相结合，为更可靠的长程语言智能体强化学习提供了可复现路径。

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习改进了推理和工具使用，然而长程语言智能体仍然会学习不支持的证据链、信念漂移以及满足终端检查的捷径动作。现有的过程奖励大多具有相关性：它们奖励类似于检索、反思或验证的步骤，但并未估计在特定干预下该步骤是否对最终验证成功做出贡献。我们提出CVT-RL，一种具有密集可验证奖励、干预有效性门控和策略条件反事实贡献（PCCC）估计器的约束策略梯度算法。删除、语义替换、证据替换和工具输出扰动定义了不同的受控干预；从冻结的参考策略中采样续写，并使用选择调整的双重稳健估计器增强优势。信念控制仅使用前缀可观察标签，而增广拉格朗日约束了不支持的声明、跳过的验证、工具篡改和不安全调用。在长上下文问答、ALFWorld、ScienceWorld以及网页/工具任务上，CVT-RL将平均任务成功率从计算匹配的非因果强化学习的71.8%和信息匹配的反事实处理基线的75.4%提高到78.9%，将证据F1从信息匹配基线的78.9提高到82.8，并将测量的黑客行为从7.2%降低到3.9%。独立的人类审计估计CVT-RL的黑客行为为4.6%，而信息匹配基线为8.1%，自适应检测器规避攻击仅将黑客行为提高到7.1%。分层自助法和混合效应检验在Holm校正后所有主要指标的p<0.01。谨慎范围的反事实信用，结合有效性门控、诊断和可验证约束，为语言智能体提供了一条可复现的路径，以实现更可靠的长程强化学习。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning and tool use, yet long-horizon language agents still learn unsupported evidence chains, belief drift, and shortcut actions that satisfy terminal checks. Existing process rewards are mostly correlational: they reward retrieval-, reflection-, or verification-like steps without estimating whether the step contributes to final verified success under a specified intervention. We propose CVT-RL, a constrained policy-gradient algorithm with dense verifiable rewards, intervention-validity gating, and a policy-conditioned counterfactual contribution (PCCC) estimator. Deletion, semantic substitution, evidence substitution, and tool-output perturbation define separate controlled interventions; continuations are sampled from a frozen reference policy, and a selection-adjusted doubly robust estimator augments the advantage. Belief control uses only prefix-observable labels, while an augmented Lagrangian constrains unsupported claims, skipped verification, tool tampering, and unsafe calls. On long-context QA, ALFWorld, ScienceWorld, and web/tool tasks, CVT-RL improves average task success from 71.8% for compute-matched non-causal RL and 75.4% for an information-matched counterfactual-process baseline to 78.9%, improves evidence F1 from 78.9 to 82.8 over the information-matched baseline, and reduces measured hacking from 7.2% to 3.9%. Independent human audit estimates 4.6% hacking for CVT-RL versus 8.1% for the information-matched baseline, and adaptive detector-evasion attacks raise hacking only to 7.1%. Stratified bootstrap and mixed-effects tests give p<0.01 after Holm correction for all primary metrics. Carefully scoped counterfactual credit, paired with validity gating, diagnostics, and verifiable constraints, provides a reproducible route toward more reliable long-horizon RL for language agents.

### [108] [Towards Efficient and Evidence-grounded Mobility Prediction with LLM-Driven Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05130v1)
*Linyao Chen,Qinlao Zhao,Zechen Li,Mingming Li,Likun Ni,Jinyu Chen,Yuhao Yao,Xuan Song,Noboru Koshizuka,Hiroki Kobayashi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出AgentMob框架，通过基于历史规律性的快速路径处理常规案例；对模糊案例，触发迭代工具使用，收集近期轨迹、历史行为、停留-移动可能性及地理证据进行自适应预测。

Original abstract: Individual-level mobility prediction is central to urban simulation, transportation planning, and policy analysis. Supervised sequence models achieve strong accuracy but require task-specific training and offer limited decision-level transparency. Recent LLM-based methods improve interpretability, yet mostly rely on static prompts and single-pass inference, limiting their ability to seek additional evidence when mobility signals are weak or conflicting. We propose \method{}, a training-free LLM-driven agent framework that formulates next-location prediction as adaptive evidence-controlled decision making. \method{} resolves routine cases through a fast path based on historical regularity, while ambiguous cases trigger iterative tool use over recent trajectories, historical behavior, stay-move likelihood, and geographical evidence. Across three mobility datasets, AgentMob achieves the strongest overall performance among training-free LLM-based methods, with GPT-5.4 reaching 71.42\% Acc@1 on BW, 33.14\% on YJMob100K, and 33.50\% on Shanghai ISP. On BW non-fast-path cases, the LLM controller improves Acc@1 from 30.65\% to 48.62\% over a same-tool statistical baseline, showing that its main benefit lies in resolving ambiguous predictions through adaptive evidence gathering. Our code is available at https://github.com/Unknown-zoo/AgentMob.

### [109] [Failed Reasoning Traces Tell You What Is Fixable (But Not by Reading Them)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05145v1)
*Nizar Islah,Istabrak Abbes,Irina Rish,Sarath Chandar,Eilif B. Muller*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 分析失败推理轨迹的分布特征用于路由和干预，可迁移到coding agent的自我改进

TL;DR: 提出三个特征从失败轨迹中提取可恢复性结构，用于聚类失败、分析后训练方法，并实现无需训练的路由规则以提升挽救率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前方法在语言模型失败时仅丢弃失败轨迹并重试，忽视了失败中蕴含的结构信息，这些信息有助于区分可恢复与不可恢复的失败。

Method: 从可用干预措施的结构中提取三个问题级轨迹特征，利用失败轨迹的分布签名（而非文本）来恢复可恢复性结构，并通过聚类和路由规则进行应用。

Result: 三个特征以84.3±4.3%准确率聚类失败（+20% over多数类基线），路由规则在Steerable-Hard子集上提升挽救率12.2%，且跨模型家族转移。

Conclusion: 失败轨迹可通过三个特征转化为诊断对象，支持测试时路由和后训练分析，无需训练或权重访问，提升了推理效率。
}

中文摘要：当后训练语言模型在推理问题上失败时，常见的测试时扩展响应是花费更多计算进行额外尝试，而失败的轨迹不再起作用。我们认为这丢弃了一个关键信号；一些失败来自不幸运的采样，更多的尝试有助于解决，而其他失败是结构性的，无论预算如何都无法通过重采样解决。我们提出，失败的轨迹编码了可恢复性结构：哪些测试时干预措施可以挽救给定失败的推理时签名。三个来自可用干预措施结构的问题级轨迹特征，从失败轨迹的分布签名（而非其文本）中恢复这种结构。它们将失败聚类为稳定区域，表征不同后训练方法的失败地形（准确率84.3±4.3%，比多数类基线高+20%），并支持一个无需训练的路由规则，在部署相关的Steerable-Hard子集（重试不足且可达有界干预的失败）上提升挽救率+12.2%。这些特征和路由规则跨两个跨家族探针转移。因此，这三个特征将失败轨迹从丢弃数据转化为诊断对象，支持测试时路由和后训练分析，无需训练时或权重空间访问。

Original abstract: When post-trained language models fail on reasoning problems, the common test-time-scaling response is to spend more compute on additional attempts, and the failed traces play no further role. We argue this discards a crucial signal; some failures come from unlucky sampling, where more rollouts help, while others are structural and resist resampling regardless of budget. We propose that failed traces encode recoverability structure: the inference-time signature of which test-time interventions can rescue a given failure. Three problem-level trajectory features, derived from the structure of available interventions, recover this structure from the distributional signature of failed rollouts, not their text. They cluster failures into stable regimes, characterize the failure topography of different post-training methods ($84.3{\pm}4.3\%$ accuracy, $+20\%$ over a majority-class baseline), and support a training-free routing rule that lifts rescue by $+12.2\%$ on the deployment-relevant Steerable-Hard subset (failures where retry is insufficient and a bounded intervention is reachable). The features and the routing rule transfer across two cross-family probes. The same three features thus convert failed traces from discarded data into a diagnostic object, supporting test-time routing and post-training analysis without training-time or weight-space access.

### [110] [Reinforcement Learning from Rich Feedback with Distributional DAgger](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05152v2)
*Rishabh Agrawal,Jacob Fein-Ashley,Paria Rashidinejad*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 从丰富反馈（包括执行轨迹）中学习，分布化DAgger，直接适用于coding agent的强化学习

TL;DR: 提出DistIL方法，利用前向交叉熵目标从丰富反馈中学习，实现单调策略改进和更好的Pass@N，在多个领域超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法仅使用单个比特的奖励信号，忽略了丰富的反馈信息；而基于反向KL或Jensen-Shannon的自蒸馏方法无法保证单调策略改进。因此需要更有效的利用反馈的方法。

Method: 基于DAgger的分布变体，使用前向交叉熵目标，该目标接受黑盒专家，通过序列级梯度将未来分歧传播回早期决策，实现信用分配。

Result: 在科学推理、编码和数学问题等领域，DistIL优于RLVR和自蒸馏强化学习基线，并改进了Pass@N。

Conclusion: 前向交叉熵目标能保证单调策略改进和遗憾界，优化教师加权成功可能性的下界，是一种更有效的利用丰富反馈的强化学习方法。

中文摘要：推理模型已经取得了快速进展，但基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）的主流方法仍然出奇地狭隘：采样许多响应，并用一个单一比特来奖励每个响应，指示最终答案是否正确。然而，许多设置提供了丰富的反馈，包括执行轨迹、工具输出、专家修正和模型自评估。我们研究如何通过经典模仿学习算法DAgger的分布变体来利用此类反馈，其中学习器可以局部访问当前策略所访问状态上的专家分布。这产生了一个简单的前向交叉熵目标，它接受黑盒专家，并且其序列级梯度通过将未来的专家-学生分歧回溯到早期决策来进行丰富的信用分配。我们表明，先前基于反向KL或Jensen-Shannon的自蒸馏目标的强化学习无法保证单调策略改进：即使专家具有更高的奖励，它们的更新也可能增加较差动作的概率。相比之下，我们表明前向交叉熵允许单调策略改进，并享有遗憾保证。我们进一步表明，我们的目标优化了教师加权成功可能性的下界，从而改进了Pass@N。在经验上，我们的方法DistIL在多个领域（科学推理、编码和解决硬数学问题）中优于RLVR和基于自蒸馏的强化学习基线。

Original abstract: Reasoning models have advanced rapidly, but the dominant reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) recipe remains surprisingly narrow: sample many responses and reward each with a single bit indicating whether the final answer is correct. Yet many settings provide rich feedback, including execution traces, tool outputs, expert corrections, and model self-evaluations. We study how to use such feedback through a distributional variant of the classic imitation learning algorithm DAgger, where the learner has local access to an expert distribution on states visited by the current policy. This yields a simple forward cross-entropy objective that admits a blackbox expert and whose sequence-level gradient {conduct rich credit assignment by propagating} future expert-student disagreement back to earlier decisions. We show that prior RL with self-distillation objectives based on reverse KL or Jensen-Shannon fail to guarantee monotonic policy improvement: even when the expert has higher reward, their updates may increase probability on worse actions. In contrast, we show that forward cross-entropy admits monotonic policy improvement and enjoys guarantees on regret. We further show that our objective optimizes a lower bound on teacher-weighted likelihood of success, leading to improved Pass@N. Empirically, our approach, DistIL, improves over RLVR and RL with self-distillation baselines across a variety of domains: scientific reasoning, coding, and solving hard mathematical problems.

</details>


### [111] [Agentic Monte Carlo: Simulating Reinforcement Learning for Black-Box Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05296v1)
*Dae Yon Hwang,Raunaq Suri,Valentin Villecroze,Anthony L. Caterini,Jesse C. Cresswell,Noël Vouitsis,Brendan Leigh Ross*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 黑盒LLM agent的蒙特卡洛优化，无需参数更新，直接相关agent推理优化

TL;DR: 提出AMC方法，利用贝叶斯推理等价性，通过顺序蒙特卡洛采样直接优化黑盒LLM代理策略，无需参数级RL训练，在AgentGym基准上取得优于GRPO的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑盒LLM代理仅提供API访问，无法进行参数级别的强化学习优化，需要一种无需修改模型参数即可优化其策略的方法。

Method: 基于RL与贝叶斯推理的等价性，将最优策略视为轨迹后验，以固定黑盒LLM代理为先验，使用顺序蒙特卡洛（SMC）通过学习价值函数来引导采样，从而近似后验分布。

Result: 在AgentGym三个环境上的实验表明，AMC显著优于提示基线，且随着测试时计算量增加，性能甚至超过GRPO。

Conclusion: AMC证明了在不修改模型参数的情况下，对黑盒LLM代理进行原则性RL风格优化的可行性，为黑盒代理的优化提供了新途径。

中文摘要：LLM代理在两种不同的状态下运行：一种是适合强化学习（RL）的开源代理，另一种是黑盒代理，其行为必须完全在测试时控制。尽管黑盒代理通常由最先进的专有LLM支持，但仅通过API访问排除了参数级别的优化，使得大多数RL方法不适用。为解决这一限制，我们转向RL与贝叶斯推理之间的已知等价性。我们提出Agentic Monte Carlo（AMC）来直接对黑盒代理的最优策略进行采样，而不是通过RL训练它。最优策略是轨迹上的后验分布，其先验我们定义为固定的黑盒LLM代理。我们采用顺序蒙特卡洛方法通过学习一个价值函数来引导代理，同时保持底层黑盒模型不变。我们在AgentGym基准测试的三个不同环境中验证了AMC，显示出相对于提示基线的显著改进，并且随着我们方法测试时计算量的增加，甚至优于群组相对策略优化（GRPO）。AMC展示了进行黑盒LLM代理的原则性RL风格优化的可行性。代码可在https://github.com/layer6ai-labs/Agentic-Monte-Carlo获取。

Original abstract: LLM agents operate in two distinct regimes: open-weight agents amenable to reinforcement learning (RL) and black-box agents whose behaviour must be controlled purely at test time. Although black-box agents are often backed by state-of-the-art proprietary LLMs, API-only access precludes parameter-level optimization, rendering most RL methods inapplicable. To address this limitation, we turn to a known equivalence between RL and Bayesian inference. We propose Agentic Monte Carlo (AMC) to directly sample from the optimal policy of a black-box agent rather than training it through RL. The optimal policy is a posterior over trajectories whose prior we define as the fixed black-box LLM agent. We employ Sequential Monte Carlo to sample from this posterior by learning a value function to steer the agent while leaving the underlying black-box model unchanged. We validate AMC on three diverse environments from the AgentGym benchmark, demonstrating significant improvements over prompting baselines and even outperforming Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) as we scale the test-time compute of our method. AMC demonstrates the feasibility of performing principled RL-style optimization of black-box LLM agents. Code is available at https://github.com/layer6ai-labs/Agentic-Monte-Carlo

</details>


### [112] [Statistically Reliable LLM-Based Ranking Evaluation via Prediction-Powered Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05308v1)
*Abhishek Divekar*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于LLM的排名评估统计方法，可迁移到agent benchmark评估

TL;DR: 提出PRECISE方法，将预测驱动推理扩展到排序评估指标，通过融合少量人工标注和大量LLM判断，无偏估计层次化指标（如Precision@K），显著降低估计误差并成功应用于生产系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有排序评估指标估计依赖大量人工标注，成本高昂；LLM判断存在偏差但可大规模获取。需要一种无偏且高效的方法结合两者来准确估计排序指标。

Method: 基于预测驱动推理（PPI）框架，针对层次化指标如Precision@K，将输出空间计算复杂度从O(2^|C|)降至O(2^K)，使得在少量人工标注下能无偏估计指标。

Result: 在ESCI基准上，30个人工标注结合Claude 3 Sonnet使Precision@4标准误差减少21%；生产系统中，用100个人工标签和2小时专家标注正确选出最佳系统变体，A/B测试证实日销售额提升407 bps。

Conclusion: PRECISE有效结合了少量人工标注和大量LLM判断，实现了排序评估指标的无偏估计，降低了标注成本，在实际系统中验证了其有效性。

中文摘要：通过PRECISE，我们将预测驱动推理扩展到从少量人工标注集和大量LLM判断集结合产生偏差校正的排序评估指标估计。PPI是证明无偏的，无论LLM判断的错误分布如何。我们使其适用于层次化指标如Precision@K，其中标注是基于文档的但指标是基于查询的，通过将输出空间计算从O(2^|C|)减少到O(2^K)。在ESCI基准测试中，用30个人工标注结合Claude 3 Sonnet判断，将Precision@4估计的标准误差从4.45降低到3.50（相对减少21%）。在一个生产系统中，我们的框架从100个人工标签和2小时的领域专家标注中正确识别了三个系统变体中最好的一个；A/B测试确认了这个排名，日销售额增加了407个基点。

Original abstract: With PRECISE, we extended Prediction-Powered Inference to produce bias-corrected estimates of ranking evaluation metrics by combining a small human-labeled set with a large LLM-judged set. PPI is provably unbiased regardless of the LLM judge's error profile. We make it applicable to hierarchical metrics like Precision@K, where annotations are per-document but the metric is per-query, by reducing the output-space computation from O(2^|C|) to O(2^K). On the ESCI benchmark, augmenting 30 human annotations with Claude 3 Sonnet judgments reduces the standard error of Precision@4 estimates from 4.45 to 3.50 (a 21% relative reduction). In a production system, our framework correctly identified the best of three system variants from 100 human labels and 2 hours of domain-expert annotation; A/B testing confirmed this ranking with +407 bps in daily sales.

</details>


### [113] [Trust, but Don't Verify: Epistemic Blind Spots in LLM Source Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05403v2)
*Rohan N. Pradhan,Steve Goley*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 揭示LLM在源评估中的认知盲点，对agent的可信度设计有参考价值

TL;DR: 语言模型在多源信息综合时无法利用其孤立情况下具备的统计伪造检测能力，而是依赖方法论-语域表示进行加权，导致对有效和捏造统计数据给出相似估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型在多源证据综合中是否评估证据质量，还是仅基于表面形式聚合，揭示其潜在的认知缺陷。

Method: 通过对比孤立检测与多源综合任务，使用六个模型（Anthropic Claude、Qwen、OLMo、OpenAI GPT-5.4）和三个领域，结合因果追踪、线性探针和组件级归因进行机制分析。

Result: 模型在多源综合中无法区分有效与捏造统计数据，权重分配由方法论-语域门控决定，数值有效性信号被抑制；提示缓解措施无效。

Conclusion: 模型存在认知对齐问题：具备检测能力但未在需要时调用，类似于偏好和安全对齐中的能力-部署脱节。

中文摘要：语言模型越来越多地充当认知代理，综合来自多个来源的证据以指导决策。它们是否评估这些证据的质量，还是仅仅基于表面呈现进行聚合，目前尚不清楚。我们表明，模型在孤立情况下具备检测捏造统计数据的能力，但在多源综合过程中并未调动这一能力，无论统计数据是捏造的还是有效的，都会产生相似的数值估计。具体而言，来源影响受一种方法论-语域门控机制支配，该机制对分析性文本的分布语域做出响应，而非对数值有效性响应：例如，统计上不可能的置信区间与有效区间获得相同的权重。这种行为分离在来自四个家族（Anthropic Claude、Qwen、OLMo 和 OpenAI GPT-5.4）的六个模型以及三个专业领域中得以复现。机制分析（包括因果追踪、线性探针和组件级归因）均指向同一解释：模型编码并因果地使用一种跨领域迁移的方法论-语域表示，而数值有效性信号（在孤立情况下可解码）在多源综合过程中被抑制至随机水平。基于提示的缓解措施（甚至是指定确切统计检查的预言清单）会导致全面怀疑而非选择性辨别，我们所检查的训练后流水线强化了这种捷径而未建立数值验证。与迎合用户偏好的谄媚不同，这种失败取决于来源是否呈现为分析可信，而非其主张是否一致。我们将此称为“认知对齐”：与偏好对齐和安全对齐类似，问题不在于能力而在于部署。

Original abstract: Language models increasingly act as epistemic proxies, synthesizing evidence from multiple sources to inform decisions. Whether they evaluate the quality of that evidence, or merely aggregate it based on surface presentation, remains poorly understood. We show that models possess the capability to detect fabricated statistics in isolation but do not recruit this capability during multi-source synthesis, producing similar numeric estimates whether the statistics are fabricated or valid. Specifically, source influence is governed by a methodology-register gate that responds to the distributional register of analytical text but not to numeric validity: for example, statistically impossible confidence intervals receive the same weight as valid ones. The behavioral dissociation replicates across six models from four families (Anthropic Claude, Qwen, OLMo, and OpenAI GPT-5.4) and three professional domains. Mechanistic analyses, including causal tracing, linear probes, and component-level attribution, converge on the same account: the model encodes and causally uses a methodology-register representation that transfers across domains, while numeric-validity signals, decodable in isolation, are suppressed to chance during multi-source synthesis. Prompting-based mitigations, even an oracle checklist naming the exact statistical checks, produce blanket skepticism rather than selective discernment, and the post-training pipelines we examine reinforce the shortcut without building numeric verification. Unlike sycophancy, which tracks user preference, this failure tracks whether a source presents as analytically credible, not whether its claims are consistent. We term this \textit{epistemic alignment}: like preference and safety alignment, the question is not capability but deployment.

</details>
